candidate_entries.push(LearningEntry::new(\n285\t                    bead_id.clone(),\n286\t                    worker.clone(),\n287\t                    bead_type.clone(),\n288\t                    text.clone(),\n289\t                    Confidence::High,\n290\t                    format!(\"reusable-pattern from {bead_id}\"),\n291\t                ));\n292\t            }\n293\t            if let Some(text) = &retro.what_worked {\n294\t                candidate_entries.push(LearningEntry::new(\n295\t                    bead_id.clone(),\n296\t                    worker.clone(),\n297\t                    bead_type.clone(),\n298\t                    text.clone(),\n299\t                    Confidence::Medium,\n300\t                    format!(\"what-worked from {bead_id}\"),\n301\t                ));\n302\t            }\n303\t            if let Some(text) = &retro.surprise {\n304\t                candidate_entries.push(LearningEntry::new(\n305\t                    bead_id.clone(),\n306\t                    worker.clone(),\n307\t                    bead_type.clone(),\n308\t                    text.clone(),\n309\t                    Confidence::Medium,\n310\t                    format!(\"surprise from {bead_id}\"),\n311\t                ));\n312\t            }\n313\t            if let Some(text) = &retro.what_didnt {\n314\t                candidate_entries.push(LearningEntry::new(\n315\t                    bead_id.clone(),\n316\t                    worker.clone(),\n317\t                    bead_type.clone(),\n318\t                    text.clone(),\n319\t                    Confidence::Low,\n320\t                    format!(\"what-didnt-work from {bead_id}\"),\n321\t                ));\n322\t            }\n323\t        }\n324\t\n325\t        // Reinforce existing entries that match any closed bead ID, then add\n326\t        // non-duplicate candidates up to max_learnings_per_run.\n327\t        for bead in &since_last {\n328\t            let _ = learnings.reinforce_entry(&bead.id);\n329\t        }\n330\t\n331\t        let mut added = 0usize;\n332\t        for candidate in candidate_entries {\n333\t            if added >= self.config.max_learnings_per_run {\n334\t                break;\n335\t            }\n336\t            // Skip if a similar entry already exists (dedup).\n337\t            let similar = learnings.find_similar(&candidate.observation);\n338\t            if !similar.is_empty() {\n339\t                // Reinforce the most similar entry instead of adding a duplicate.\n340\t                let most_similar_id = similar[0].bead_id.clone();\n341\t                let _ = learnings.reinforce_entry(&most_similar_id);\n342\t                continue;\n343\t            }\n344\t            learnings.add_entry(candidate)?;\n345\t            added += 1;\n346\t        }\n347\t        summary.learnings_added = added;\n348\t\n349\t        // Promote high-reinforcement entries to skill files.\n350\t        let promoted = self.promote_to_skills(learnings.entries())?;\n351\t        summary.skills_promoted = promoted;\n352\t\n353\t        // Promote cross-workspace patterns to global learnings.\n354\t        let global_promoted = self.promote_cross_workspace_patterns(&learnings)?;\n355\t        summary.global_learnings_promoted = global_promoted;\n356\t\n357\t        // ── Phase 4: Prune ────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n358\t        let pruned = learnings.prune_stale()?;\n359\t        summary.learnings_pruned = pruned;\n360\t\n361\t        // Enforce max_learnings cap.\n362\t        let over_limit = learnings.consolidate(self.config.max_learnings)?;\n363\t        summary.learnings_pruned += over_limit;\n364\t\n365\t        // Persist updated state.\n366\t        let new_state = ReflectState {\n367\t            last_consolidation: Utc::now(),\n368\t            beads_at_last_consolidation: total_closed,\n369\t        };\n370\t        new_state.save(&self.state_dir)?;\n371\t\n372\t        let _ = self.telemetry.emit(EventKind::ReflectConsolidated {\n373\t            learnings_added: summary.learnings_added,\n374\t            learnings_pruned: summary.learnings_pruned,\n375\t            skills_promoted: summary.skills_promoted,\n376\t            beads_processed: summary.beads_processed,\n377\t        });\n378\t\n379\t        tracing::info!(\n380\t            learnings_added = summary.learnings_added,\n381\t            learnings_pruned = summary.learnings_pruned,\n382\t            skills_promoted = summary.skills_promoted,\n383\t            beads_processed = summary.beads_processed,\n384\t            \"reflect: consolidation complete\"\n385\t        );\n386\t\n387\t        Ok(summary)\n388\t    }\n389\t\n390\t    // ── Helpers ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n391\t\n392\t    /// Read all closed beads from issues.jsonl.\n393\t    fn read_closed_beads(&self, issues_path: &Path) -> Result<Vec<ClosedBeadRecord>> {\n394\t        let content = std::fs::read_to_string(issues_path)\n395\t            .with_context(|| format!(\"failed to read {}\", issues_path.display()))?;\n396\t\n397\t        let mut beads = Vec::new();\n398\t        for (line_no, line) in content.lines().enumerate() {\n399\t            let line = line.trim();\n400\t parse issues.jsonl line\");\n408\t                }\n409\t            }\n410\t        }\n411\t        Ok(beads)\n412\t    }\n413\t\n414\t    /// Infer bead type from labels in the closed bead record.\n415\t    fn infer_bead_type_from_id(&self, bead_id: &str, all_closed: &[ClosedBeadRecord]) -> BeadType {\n416\t        let record = all_closed.iter().find(|b| b.id == bead_id);\n417\t        if let Some(rec) = record {\n418\t            for label in &rec.labels {\n419\t                if let Some(bt) = BeadType::from_str(label) {\n420\t                    return bt;\n421\t                }\n422\t            }\n423\t        }\n424\t        BeadType::Other\n425\t    }\n426\t\n427\t    /// Infer worker from the assignee field of the closed bead record.\n428\t    fn infer_worker_from_id(&self, bead_id: &str, all_closed: &[ClosedBeadRecord]) -> String {\n429\t        all_closed\n430\t            .iter()\n431\t            .find(|b| b.id == bead_id)\n432\t            .and_then(|b| b.assignee.clone())\n433\t            .unwrap_or_else(|| \"unknown\".to_string())\n434\t    }\n435\t\n436\t    /// Promote learning entries with reinforcement_count >= 3 to skill files.\n437\t    ///\n438\t    /// Creates `.beads/skills/<slug>.md` for each promoted entry.\n439\t    /// Returns the number of skills created this run.\n440\t    fn promote_to_skills(&self, set of already-promoted bead IDs to avoid re-promoting.\n445\t        let already_promoted = self.read_promoted_ids(&skills_dir);\n446\t\n447\t        for entry in entries {\n448\t            if promoted >= self.config.max_skills_per_run {\n449\t                break;\n450\t            }\n451\t            if entry.reinforcement_count < 3 {\n452\t                continue;\n453\t            }\n454\t            if already_promoted.contains(&entry.bead_id) {\n455\t                continue;\n456\t            }\n457\t\n458\t            match self.write_skill_file(&skills_dir, entry) {\n459\t                Ok(()) => promoted += 1,\n460\t                Err(e) => {\n461\t                    tracing::warn!(bead_id = %entry.bead_id, error = %e, \"reflect: failed to write skill file\");\n462\t                }\n463\t            }\n464\t        }\n465\t\n466\t        Ok(promoted)\n467\t    }\n468\t\n469\t    /// Read the set of bead IDs that have already been promoted to std::collections::HashSet::new()\n476\t            }\n477\t        }\n478\t    }\n479\t\n480\t    /// Scan known workspaces for learnings that match entries in the current workspace,\n481\t    /// promoting matches (cross-workspace patterns) to the global learnings file.\n482\t    ///\n483\t    /// An entry is promoted when a similar observation appears in at least one other\n484\t    /// known workspace. Returns the number of entries promoted this run.\n485\t    fn promote_cross_workspace_patterns(&self, learnings: &LearningsFile) -> Result<usize> {\n486\t        // Skip when not configured.\n487\t        if self.global_learnings_path.as_os_str().is_empty() || self.known_workspaces.is_empty() {\n488\t            return Ok(0);\n489\t        }\n490\t\n491\t        let mut global = GlobalLearningsFile::load(&self.global_learnings_path)?;\n492\t\n493\t        // Load learnings files for all known workspaces, skipping failures.\n494\t        let mut other_learnings: Vec<LearningsFile> = Vec::new();\n495\t        for ws in &self.known_workspaces {\n496\t            match LearningsFile::load(ws) {\n497\t                Ok(lf) if !lf.entries().is_empty() =>                       error = %e,\n503\t                        \"reflect: failed to load learnings for cross-workspace scan\"\n504\t                    );\n505\t                }\n506\t            }\n507\t        }\n508\t\n509\t        if other_learnings.is_empty() {\n510\t            return Ok(0);\n511\t        }\n512\t\n513\t        let mut promoted = 0usize;\n514\t\n515\t        for entry in        .any(|other| !other.find_similar(&entry.observation).is_empty());\n520\t\n521\t            if !appears_in_other {\n522\t                continue;\n523\t            }\n524\t\n525\t            if global.promote(entry.clone(), self.max_global_learnings) {\n526\t                promoted += 1;\n527\t                tracing::info!(\n528\t                    bead_id = %entry.bead_id,\n529\t                    observation = %entry.observation,\n530\t                    \"reflect: promoted cross-workspace learning to global\"\n531\t                );\n532\t            }\n533\t        }\n534\t\n535\t        if promoted > 0 {\n536\t            global.write()?;\n537\t        }\n538\t\n539\t        Ok(promoted)\n540\t    }\n541\t\n542\t    /// Write a skill file for a promoted learning entry (YAML frontmatter format).\n543\t    fn write_skill_file(&self, skills_dir: &Path, entry: &LearningEntry) -> Result<()> {\n544\t        std::fs::create_dir_all(skills_dir)\n545\t            .with_context(|| format!(\"failed to create skills dir: {}\", skills_dir.display()))?;\n546\t\n547\t        let slug = slugify(&entry.observation);\n548\t        let filename = Utilities\n605\t// ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n606\t\n607\t/// Create a URL-safe slug from a string.\n608\tfn slugify(s: &str) -> String {\n609\t    s.to_lowercase()\n610\t        .chars()\n611\t        .map(|c| if c.is_alphanumeric() { c } else { '-' })\n612\t        .collect::<String>()\n613\t        .split('-')\n614\t        .filter(|s| !s.is_empty())\n615\t        .collect::<Vec<_>>()\n616\t        .join(\"-\")\n617\t}\n618\t\n619\t/// Truncate a string to at most `max_chars` characters.\n620\tfn truncate(s: &str, max_chars: usize) -> &str {\n621\t    if s.len() <= max_chars {\n622\t        s\n623\t    } else {\n624\t        &s[..max_chars]\n625\t    }\n626\t}\n627\t\n628\t// Reflect strand: meta-analysis and learning consolidation.\n//!\n//! Strand 7 in the waterfall. Runs after all other strands return NoWork.\n//! This is the last productive strategy before giving up — meta-analysis\n//! only runs when there is genuinely nothing else to do.\n//!\n//! KAIROS-inspired four-phase cycle:\n//! 1. **Orient** — read current learnings.md and existing skills, check sizes.\n//! 2. **Gather** — read bead close bodies from issues.jsonl since last\n//!    consolidation; read traces for failed beads.\n//! 3. **Consolidate** — extract retrospective blocks, identify cross-bead\n//!    patterns, merge into learnings.md, deduplicate, resolve contradictions.\n//!    Promote learnings with reinforcement_count ≥ 3 to skill files.\n//! 4. **Prune** — remove entries older than `learning_retention_days` days\n//!    without reinforcement, compress similar entries, enforce `max_learnings`.\n//!\n//! Entry conditions (checked before running):\n//! - `strands.reflect.enabled` is true\n//! - 10+ beads closed since last consolidation (configurable)\n//! - 24+ hours since last consolidation (configurable cooldown)\n//!\n//! Guardrails:\n//! - Max `max_learnings_per_run` new learnings added per run\n//! - Max `max_skills_per_run` skill files created/updated per run\n//! - CLAUDE.md is read-only — never written\n//!\n//! Depends on: `config`, `learning`, `telemetry`, `types`.\n\nuse std::path::{Path, PathBuf};\n\nuse anyhow::{Context, Result};\nuse chrono::{DateTime, Utc};\nuse serde::{Deserialize, Serialize};\n\nuse crate::bead_store::BeadStore;\nuse crate::config::ReflectConfig;\nuse crate::learning::{\n    BeadType, Confidence, GlobalLearningsFile, LearningEntry, LearningsFile, Retrospective,\n};\nuse crate::skill::{render_skill_file, SkillFrontmatter, SkillLibrary};\nuse crate::telemetry::{EventKind, Telemetry};\nuse crate::types::{StrandError, StrandResult};\n\n// ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n// State persistence\n// ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\n/// Persisted state for the Reflect strand.\n#[derive(Debug, Serialize, Deserialize)]\nstruct ReflectState {\n    /// Timestamp of the last successful consolidation.\n    last_consolidation: DateTime<Utc>,\n    /// Total closed beads at the time of last consolidation.\n    beads_at_last_consolidation: u64,\n}\n\nimpl ReflectState {\n    fn load(state_dir: &Path) -> Result<Option<Self>> {\n        let path = state_dir.join(\"reflect_state.json\");\n        if !path.exists() {\n            return Ok(None);\n        }\n        let content = std::fs::read_to_string(&path)\n            .with_context(|| format!(\"failed to read reflect state: {}\", path.display()))?;\n        let state: ReflectState =\n            serde_json::from_str(&content).with_context(|| \"failed to parse reflect state\")?;\n        Ok(Some(state))\n    }\n\n    fn save(&self, state_dir: &Path) -> Result<()> {\n        std::fs::create_dir_all(state_dir)\n            .with_context(|| format!(\"failed to create state dir: {}\", state_dir.display()))?;\n        let path = state_dir.join(\"reflect_state.json\");\n        let content = serde_json::to_string_pretty(self)?;\n        std::fs::write(&path, content)\n            .with_context(|| format!(\"failed to write reflect state: {}\", path.display()))?;\n        Ok(())\n    }\n}\n\n// ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n// Bead record (minimal, parsed from issues.jsonl)\n// ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\n/// Minimal closed-bead record read from issues.jsonl.\n#[derive(Debug, Deserialize)]\nstruct ClosedBeadRecord {\n    id: String,\n    status: String,\n    close_reason: Option<String>,\n    closed_at: Option<DateTime<Utc>>,\n    assignee: Option<String>,\n    #[serde(default)]\n    labels: Vec<String>,\n}\n\n// ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n// Summary\n// ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\n/// Work performed during one Reflect cycle.\n#[derive(Debug, Default)]\npub struct ReflectSummary {\n    pub beads_processed: usize,\n    pub learnings_added: usize,\n    pub learnings_pruned: usize,\n    pub skills_promoted: usize,\n    /// Number of learnings promoted to the global learnings file.\n    pub global_learnings_promoted: usize,\n}\n\n// ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n// Strand\n// ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\n/// The Reflect strand — meta-analysis and learning consolidation.\npub struct ReflectStrand {\n    config: ReflectConfig,\n    workspace: PathBuf,\n    state_dir: PathBuf,\n    telemetry: Telemetry,\n    /// Other workspaces to scan for cross-workspace patterns.\n    known_workspaces: Vec<PathBuf>,\n    /// Path to the global learnings file.\n    global_learnings_path: PathBuf,\n    /// Maximum entries in the global learnings file.\n    max_global_learnings: usize,\n}\n\nimpl ReflectStrand {\n    /// Create a new ReflectStrand.\n    ///\n    /// - `config`: reflect strand configuration\n    /// - `workspace`: workspace root (where `.beads/` lives)\n    /// - `state_dir`: directory for persisting reflect state (`~/.needle/state/reflect/`)\n    /// - `telemetry`: telemetry emitter\n    pub fn new(\n        config: ReflectConfig,\n        workspace: PathBuf,\n        state_dir: PathBuf,\n        telemetry: Telemetry,\n    ) -> Self {\n        ReflectStrand {\n            config,\n            workspace,\n            state_dir,\n            telemetry,\n            known_workspaces: Vec::new(),\n            global_learnings_path: PathBuf::new(),\n            max_global_learnings: 40,\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Configure cross-workspace detection and global learnings promotion.\n    ///\n    /// - `known_workspaces`: other workspace paths to check for matching patterns\n    /// - `global_learnings_path`: path to `~/.config/needle/global-learnings.md`\n    /// - `max_global_learnings`: cap on total entries in the global file (default: 40)\n    pub fn with_global(\n        mut self,\n        known_workspaces: Vec<PathBuf>,\n        global_learnings_path: PathBuf,\n        max_global_learnings: usize,\n    ) -> Self {\n        self.known_workspaces = known_workspaces;\n        self.global_learnings_path = global_learnings_path;\n        self.max_global_learnings = max_global_learnings;\n        self\n    }\n\n    /// Run the four-phase consolidation cycle.\n    ///\n    /// `force` bypasses cooldown and minimum bead threshold checks (used by\n    /// the `needle reflect` CLI command).\n    pub fn consolidate(&self, force: bool) -> Result<ReflectSummary> {\n        // ── Phase 1: Orient ───────────────────────────────────────────────────\n        let state = ReflectState::load(&self.state_dir)?;\n\n        let issues_path = self.workspace.join(\".beads\").join(\"issues.jsonl\");\n        if !issues_path.exists() {\n            tracing::debug!(\"reflect: no issues.jsonl found, skipping\");\n            return Ok(ReflectSummary::default());\n        }\n\n        // Count total closed beads and collect those since last consolidation.\n        let all_closed = self.read_closed_beads(&issues_path)?;\n        let total_closed = all_closed.len() as u64;\n\n        let since_last: Vec<&ClosedBeadRecord> = match &state {\n            Some(s) => all_closed\n                .iter()\n                .filter(|b| {\n                    b.closed_at\n                        .map(|t| t > s.last_consolidation)\n                        .unwrap_or(false)\n                })\n                .collect(),\n            None => all_closed.iter().collect(),\n        };\n\n        let beads_since = since_last.len();\n\n        if !force {\n            // Check minimum bead threshold.\n            if beads_since < self.config.min_beads_since_last {\n                tracing::debug!(\n                    beads_since,\n                    threshold = self.config.min_beads_since_last,\n                    \"reflect: below minimum bead threshold, skipping\"\n                );\n                let _ = self.telemetry.emit(EventKind::ReflectSkipped {\n                    reason: format!(\n                        \"only {} beads closed since last consolidation (need {})\",\n                        beads_since, self.config.min_beads_since_last\n                    ),\n                });\n                return Ok(ReflectSummary::default());\n            }\n\n            // Check cooldown.\n            if let Some(s) = &state {\n                let hours_since = (Utc::now() - s.last_consolidation).num_hours() as u64;\n                if hours_since < self.config.cooldown_hours {\n                    tracing::debug!(\n                        hours_since,\n                        cooldown = self.config.cooldown_hours,\n                        \"reflect: cooldown not elapsed, skipping\"\n                    );\n                    let _ = self.telemetry.emit(EventKind::ReflectSkipped {\n                        reason: format!(\n                            \"cooldown not elapsed ({}/{}h)\",\n                            hours_since, self.config.cooldown_hours\n                        ),\n                    });\n                    return Ok(ReflectSummary::default());\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        let _ = self.telemetry.emit(EventKind::ReflectStarted {\n            beads_since_last: beads_since,\n        });\n\n        tracing::info!(beads_since, force, \"reflect: starting consolidation cycle\");\n\n        // ── Phase 2: Gather ───────────────────────────────────────────────────\n        let mut retro_entries: Vec<(String, Retrospective)> = Vec::new();\n\n        for bead in &since_last {\n            if let Some(reason) = &bead.close_reason {\n                match Retrospective::parse_from_close_body(reason) {\n                    Ok(Some(retro)) if retro.is_meaningful() => {\n                        retro_entries.push((bead.id.clone(), retro));\n                    }\n                    Ok(_) => {}\n                    Err(e) => {\n                        tracing::warn!(bead_id = %bead.id, error = %e, \"failed to parse retrospective\");\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        tracing::debug!(\n            retro_count = retro_entries.len(),\n            \"reflect: gathered retrospectives\"\n        );\n\n        // ── Phase 3: Consolidate ──────────────────────────────────────────────\n        let mut learnings = LearningsFile::load(&self.workspace)?;\n        let mut summary = ReflectSummary {\n            beads_processed: beads_since,\n            ..Default::default()\n        };\n\n        // Extract learning entries from retrospectives.\n        let mut candidate_entries: Vec<LearningEntry> = Vec::new();\n\n        for (bead_id, retro) in &retro_entries {\n            // Determine bead type from labels if available.\n            let bead_type = self.infer_bead_type_from_id(bead_id, &all_closed);\n            let worker = self.infer_worker_from_id(bead_id, &all_closed);\n\n            if let Some(text) = &retro.reusable_pattern {\n                candidate_entries.push(LearningEntry::new(\n                    bead_id.clone(),\n                    worker.clone(),\n                    bead_type.clone(),\n                    text.clone(),\n                    Confidence::High,\n                    format!(\"reusable-pattern from {bead_id}\"),\n                ));\n            }\n            if let Some(text) = &retro.what_worked {\n                candidate_entries.push(LearningEntry::new(\n                    bead_id.clone(),\n                    worker.clone(),\n                    bead_type.clone(),\n                    text.clone(),\n                    Confidence::Medium,\n                    format!(\"what-worked from {bead_id}\"),\n                ));\n            }\n            if let Some(text) = &retro.surprise {\n                candidate_entries.push(LearningEntry::new(\n                    bead_id.clone(),\n                    worker.clone(),\n                    bead_type.clone(),\n                    text.clone(),\n                    Confidence::Medium,\n                    format!(\"surprise from {bead_id}\"),\n                ));\n            }\n            if let Some(text) = &retro.what_didnt {\n                candidate_entries.push(LearningEntry::new(\n                    bead_id.clone(),\n                    worker.clone(),\n                    bead_type.clone(),\n                    text.clone(),\n                    Confidence::Low,\n                    format!(\"what-didnt-work from {bead_id}\"),\n                ));\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Reinforce existing entries that match any closed bead ID, then add\n        // non-duplicate candidates up to max_learnings_per_run.\n        for bead in &since_last {\n            let _ = learnings.reinforce_entry(&bead.id);\n        }\n\n        let mut added = 0usize;\n        for candidate in candidate_entries {\n            if added >= self.config.max_learnings_per_run {\n                break;\n            }\n            // Skip if a similar entry already exists (dedup).\n            let similar = learnings.find_similar(&candidate.observation);\n            if !similar.is_empty() {\n                // Reinforce the most similar entry instead of adding a duplicate.\n                let most_similar_id = similar[0].bead_id.clone();\n                let _ = learnings.reinforce_entry(&most_similar_id);\n                continue;\n            }\n            learnings.add_entry(candidate)?;\n            added += 1;\n        }\n        summary.learnings_added = added;\n\n        // Promote high-reinforcement entries to skill files.\n        let promoted = self.promote_to_skills(learnings.entries())?;\n        summary.skills_promoted = promoted;\n\n        // Promote cross-workspace patterns to global learnings.\n        let global_promoted = self.promote_cross_workspace_patterns(&learnings)?;\n        summary.global_learnings_promoted = global_promoted;\n\n        // ── Phase 4: Prune ────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n        let pruned = learnings.prune_stale()?;\n        summary.learnings_pruned = pruned;\n\n        // Enforce max_learnings cap.\n        let over_limit = learnings.consolidate(self.config.max_learnings)?;\n        summary.learnings_pruned += over_limit;\n\n        // Persist updated state.\n        let new_state = ReflectState {\n            last_consolidation: Utc::now(),\n            beads_at_last_consolidation: total_closed,\n        };\n        new_state.save(&self.state_dir)?;\n\n        let _ = self.telemetry.emit(EventKind::ReflectConsolidated {\n            learnings_added: summary.learnings_added,\n            learnings_pruned: summary.learnings_pruned,\n            skills_promoted: summary.skills_promoted,\n            beads_processed: summary.beads_processed,\n        });\n\n        tracing::info!(\n            learnings_added = summary.learnings_added,\n            learnings_pruned = summary.learnings_pruned,\n            skills_promoted = summary.skills_promoted,\n            beads_processed = summary.beads_processed,\n            \"reflect: consolidation complete\"\n        );\n\n        Ok(summary)\n    }\n\n    // ── Helpers ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\n    /// Read all closed beads from issues.jsonl.\n    fn read_closed_beads(&self, issues_path: &Path) -> Result<Vec<ClosedBeadRecord>> {\n        let content = std::fs::read_to_string(issues_path)\n            .with_context(|| format!(\"failed to read {}\", issues_path.display()))?;\n\n        let mut beads = Vec::new();\n        for (line_no, line) in content.lines().enumerate() {\n            let line = line.trim();\n            if line.is_empty() {\n                continue;\n            }\n            match serde_json::from_str::<ClosedBeadRecord>(line) {\n                Ok(record) if record.status == \"closed\" => beads.push(record),\n                Ok(_) => {}\n                Err(e) => {\n                    tracing::warn!(line = line_no + 1, error = %e, \"reflect: failed to parse issues.jsonl line\");\n                }\n            }\n        }\n        Ok(beads)\n    }\n\n    /// Infer bead type from labels in the closed bead record.\n    fn infer_bead_type_from_id(&self, bead_id: &str, all_closed: &[ClosedBeadRecord]) -> BeadType {\n        let record = all_closed.iter().find(|b| b.id == bead_id);\n        if let Some(rec) = record {\n            for label in &rec.labels {\n                if let Some(bt) = BeadType::from_str(label) {\n                    return bt;\n                }\n            }\n        }\n        BeadType::Other\n    }\n\n    /// Infer worker from the assignee field of the closed bead record.\n    fn infer_worker_from_id(&self, bead_id: &str, all_closed: &[ClosedBeadRecord]) -> String {\n        all_closed\n            .iter()\n            .find(|b| b.id == bead_id)\n            .and_then(|b| b.assignee.clone())\n            .unwrap_or_else(|| \"unknown\".to_string())\n    }\n\n    /// Promote learning entries with reinforcement_count >= 3 to skill files.\n    ///\n    /// Creates `.beads/skills/<slug>.md` for each promoted entry.\n    /// Returns the number of skills created this run.\n    fn promote_to_skills(&self, entries: &[LearningEntry]) -> Result<usize> {\n        let skills_dir = self.workspace.join(\".beads\").join(\"skills\");\n        let mut promoted = 0usize;\n\n        // Build set of already-promoted bead IDs to avoid re-promoting.\n        let already_promoted = self.read_promoted_ids(&skills_dir);\n\n        for entry in entries {\n            if promoted >= self.config.max_skills_per_run {\n                break;\n            }\n            if entry.reinforcement_count < 3 {\n                continue;\n            }\n            if already_promoted.contains(&entry.bead_id) {\n                continue;\n            }\n\n            match self.write_skill_file(&skills_dir, entry) {\n                Ok(()) => promoted += 1,\n                Err(e) => {\n                    tracing::warn!(bead_id = %entry.bead_id, error = %e, \"reflect: failed to write skill file\");\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        Ok(promoted)\n    }\n\n    /// Read the set of bead IDs that have already been promoted to skills.\n    fn read_promoted_ids(&self, _skills_dir: &Path) -> std::collections::HashSet<String> {\n        match SkillLibrary::load(&self.workspace) {\n            Ok(lib) => lib.promoted_source_beads(),\n            Err(e) => {\n                tracing::warn!(error = %e, \"reflect: failed to load skill library for promoted IDs\");\n                std::collections::HashSet::new()\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Scan known workspaces for learnings that match entries in the current workspace,\n    /// promoting matches (cross-workspace patterns) to the global learnings file.\n    ///\n    /// An entry is promoted when a similar observation appears in at least one other\n    /// known workspace. Returns the number of entries promoted this run.\n    fn promote_cross_workspace_patterns(&self, learnings: &LearningsFile) -> Result<usize> {\n        // Skip when not configured.\n        if self.global_learnings_path.as_os_str().is_empty() || self.known_workspaces.is_empty() {\n            return Ok(0);\n        }\n\n        let mut global = GlobalLearningsFile::load(&self.global_learnings_path)?;\n\n        // Load learnings files for all known workspaces, skipping failures.\n        let mut other_learnings: Vec<LearningsFile> = Vec::new();\n        for ws in &self.known_workspaces {\n            match LearningsFile::load(ws) {\n                Ok(lf) if !lf.entries().is_empty() => other_learnings.push(lf),\n                Ok(_) => {}\n                Err(e) => {\n                    tracing::warn!(\n                        workspace = %ws.display(),\n                        error = %e,\n                        \"reflect: failed to load learnings for cross-workspace scan\"\n                    );\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        if other_learnings.is_empty() {\n            return Ok(0);\n        }\n\n        let mut promoted = 0usize;\n\n        for entry in learnings.entries() {\n            // Check if any other workspace has a similar observation.\n            let appears_in_other = other_learnings\n                .iter()\n                .any(|other| !other.find_similar(&entry.observation).is_empty());\n\n            if !appears_in_other {\n                continue;\n            }\n\n            if global.promote(entry.clone(), self.max_global_learnings) {\n                promoted += 1;\n                tracing::info!(\n                    bead_id = %entry.bead_id,\n                    observation = %entry.observation,\n                    \"reflect: promoted cross-workspace learning to global\"\n                );\n            }\n        }\n\n        if promoted > 0 {\n            global.write()?;\n        }\n\n        Ok(promoted)\n    }\n\n    /// Write a skill file for a promoted learning entry (YAML frontmatter format).\n    fn write_skill_file(&self, skills_dir: &Path, entry: &LearningEntry) -> Result<()> {\n        std::fs::create_dir_all(skills_dir)\n            .with_context(|| format!(\"failed to create skills dir: {}\", skills_dir.display()))?;\n\n        let slug = slugify(&entry.observation);\n        let filename = format!(\"{}-{}.md\", &slug[..slug.len().min(40)], &entry.bead_id);\n        let path = skills_dir.join(&filename);\n\n        let frontmatter = SkillFrontmatter {\n            task_types: vec![entry.bead_type.as_str().to_string()],\n            labels: vec![],\n            success_count: 0,\n            last_used: None,\n            source_beads: vec![entry.bead_id.clone()],\n        };\n\n        let body = format!(\n            \"## {}\\n\\n{}\\n\\n**Worker:** {}\\n**Source:** {}\\n\",\n            truncate(&entry.observation, 60),\n            entry.observation,\n            entry.worker,\n            entry.source,\n        );\n\n        let content = render_skill_file(&frontmatter, &body)\n            .with_context(|| format!(\"failed to render skill file: {filename}\"))?;\n\n        std::fs::write(&path, content)\n            .with_context(|| format!(\"failed to write skill file: {}\", path.display()))?;\n\n        tracing::info!(\n            bead_id = %entry.bead_id,\n            file = %filename,\n            reinforcement_count = entry.reinforcement_count,\n            \"reflect: promoted learning to skill file\"\n        );\n        Ok(())\n    }\n}\n\n#[async_trait::async_trait]\nimpl super::Strand for ReflectStrand {\n    fn name(&self) -> &str {\n        \"reflect\"\n    }\n\n    async fn evaluate(&self, _store: &dyn BeadStore) -> StrandResult {\n        if !self.config.enabled {\n            return StrandResult::NoWork;\n        }\n\n        match self.consolidate(false) {\n            Ok(_) => StrandResult::NoWork,\n            Err(e) => StrandResult::Error(StrandError::ConfigError(format!(\n                \"reflect consolidation failed: {e}\"\n            ))),\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n// ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n// Utilities\n// ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\n/// Create a URL-safe slug from a string.\nfn slugify(s: &str) -> String {\n    s.to_lowercase()\n        .chars()\n        .map(|c| if c.is_alphanumeric() { c } else { '-' })\n        .collect::<String>()\n        .split('-')\n        .filter(|s| !s.is_empty())\n        .collect::<Vec<_>>()\n        .join(\"-\")\n}\n\n/// Truncate a string to at most `max_chars` characters.\nfn truncate(s: &str, max_chars: usize) -> &str {\n    if s.len() <= max_chars {\n        s\n    } else {\n }\n71\t\n72\t    /// Persist state to disk.\n73\t    fn save(&self, path: &Path) -> Result<()> {\n74\t        if let Some(parent) = path.parent() {\n75\t            std::fs::create_dir_all(parent)\n76\t                .with_context(|| format!(\"failed to create state dir: {}\", parent.display()))?;\n77\t        }\n78\t        let data = serde_json::to_string_pretty(self).context(\"failed to serialize weave state\")?;\n79\t        std::fs::write(path, data)\n80\t            .with_context(|| format!(\"failed to write weave state: {}\", path.display()))\n81\t    }\n82\t\n83\t    /// Check if cooldown has elapsed since last run.\n84\t    fn cooldown_elapsed(&self, cooldown_hours: u64) -> bool {\n85\t        match self.last_run {\n86\t            None => true,\n87\t            Some(last) => {\n88\t                let elapsed = Utc::now().signed_duration_since(last);\n89\t                elapsed.num_hours() >= cooldown_hours as i64\n90\t            }\n91\t        }\n92\t    }\n93\t\n94\t    /// Check if a title was already seen (dedup).\n95\t    fn is_duplicate(&self, title: &str) -> bool {\n96\t        self.seen_titles.contains(&title.to_lowercase())\n97\t    }\n98\t\n99\t    /// Record a title as seen.\n100\t    fn mark_seen(&mut self, title: &str) {\n101\t        self.seen_titles.insert(title.to_lowercase());\n102\t    }\n103\t}\n104\t\n105\t// ─── WeaveStrand ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n106\t\n107\t/// The Weave strand — analyzes documentation gaps and creates beads.\n108\tpub struct WeaveStrand {\n109\t    config: WeaveConfig,\n110\t    workspace: PathBuf,\n111\t    state_dir: PathBuf,\n112\t    agent: Box<dyn WeaveAgent>,\n113\t}\n114\t\n115\timpl WeaveStrand {\n116\t    /// Create a new WeaveStrand.\n117\t    ///\n118\t    /// `state_dir` is the base directory for weave state files\n119\t    /// (e.g., `~/.needle/state/weave/`).\n120\t    pub fn new(\n121\t        config: WeaveConfig,\n122\t        workspace: PathBuf,\n123\t        state_dir: PathBuf,\n124\t        agent: Box<dyn WeaveAgent>,\n125\t    ) -> Self {\n126\t        WeaveStrand {\n127\t            config,\n128\t            workspace,\n129\t            state_dir,\n130\t            agent,\n131\t        }\n132\t    }\n133\t\n134\t    /// Compute the state file path for a workspace.\n135\t    ///\n136\t    /// Uses a SHA-256 hash of the workspace path to create a unique filename.\n137\t    fn state_file_path(&self) -> PathBuf {\n138\t        let hash = workspace_hash(&self.workspace);\n139\t        self.state_dir.join(format!(\"{hash}.json\"))\n140\t    }\n141\t\n142\t    /// Check if this workspace is excluded from weave.\n143\t    fn is_workspace_excluded(&self) -> bool {\n144\t        self.config\n145\t            .exclude_workspaces\n146\t            .iter()\n147\t            .any(|excluded| excluded == &self.workspace)\n148\t    }\n149\t\n150\t    /// Discover documentation files in the workspace using configured patterns.\n151\t    fn discover_doc_files(&self) -> Vec<PathBuf> {\n152\t        let mut files = Vec::new();\n153\t        for pattern in &self.config.doc_patterns {\n154\t            let full_pattern = self.workspace.join(pattern).display().to_string();\n155\t            if let Ok(entries) = glob::glob(&full_pattern) {\n156\t                for entry in entries.flatten() {\n157\t                    if entry.is_file() && !files.contains(&entry) {\n158\t                        files.push(entry);\n159\t                    }\n160\t                }\n161\t            }\n162\t        }\n163\t        files.sort();\n164\t        files\n165\t    }\n166\t\n167\t    /// Format documentation files into a string for the prompt.\n168\t    fn format_doc_files(files: &[PathBuf], workspace: &Path) -> String {\n169\t        if files.is_empty() {\n170\t            return \"(no documentation files found)\".to_string();\n171\t        }\n172\t\n173\t        let mut sections = Vec::new();\n174\t        for file in files {\n175\t            let rel_path = file\n176\t                .strip_prefix(workspace)\n177\t                .unwrap_or(file)\n178\t                .display()\n179\t                .to_string();\n180\t            match std::fs::read_to_string(file) {\n181\t                Ok(content) => {\n182\t                    sections.push(format!(\"### {rel_path}\\n\\n{}\", content.trim_end()));\n183\t                }\n184\t                Err(_) => {\n185\t                    sections.push(format!(\"### {rel_path}\\n\\n(failed to read)\"));\n186\t                }\n187\t            }\n188\t        }\n189\t        sections.join(\"\\n\\n\")\n190\t    }\n191\t\n192\t    /// Format existing beads into a string for the prompt.\n193\t    fn format_existing_beads(beads: &[crate::types::Bead]) -> String {\n194\t        if beads.is_empty() {\n195\t            return \"(no open beads)\".to_string();\n196\t        }\n197\t\n198\t        beads\n199\t            .iter()\n200\t            .map(|b| {\n201\t                let title = &b.title;\n202\t                let id = b.id.as_ref();\n203\t                let priority = b.priority;\n204\t                format!(\"- [{id}] P{priority}: {title}\")\n205\t            })\n206\t            .collect::<Vec<_>>()\n207\t            .join(\"\\n\")\n208\t    }\n209\t\n210\t    /// Parse the agent response into proposed beads.\n211\t    ///\n212\t    /// The agent may return:\n213\t    /// - `NO_GAPS` — no gaps found\n214\t    /// - A JSON array of proposed beads\n215\t    /// - A JSON object with a `beads` field containing an array\n216\t    pub fn parse_agent_response(response: &str) -> Result<Vec<ProposedBead>> {\n217\t        let trimmed = response.trim();\n218\t\n219\t        // Check for NO_GAPS sentinel.\n220\t        if trimmed.contains(\"NO_GAPS\") {\n221\t            return Ok(vec![]);\n222\t        }\n223\t\n224\t        // Try parsing as a JSON array directly.\n225\t        if let Ok(beads) = serde_json::from_str::<Vec<ProposedBead>>(trimmed) {\n226\t            return Ok(beads);\n227\t        }\n228\t\n229\t        // Try extracting JSON from markdown code fences.\n230\t        let json_str = extract_json_block(trimmed).unwrap_or(trimmed);\n231\t\n232\t        // Try as array.\n233\t        if let Ok(beads) = serde_json::from_str::<Vec<ProposedBead>>(json_str) {\n234\t            return Ok(beads);\n235\t        }\n236\t\n237\t        // Try as object with \"beads\" field.\n238\t        if let Ok(obj) = serde_json::from_str::<serde_json::Value>(json_str) {\n239\t            if let Some(arr) = obj.get(\"beads\").and_then(|v| v.as_array()) {\n240\t                let beads: Vec<ProposedBead> = arr\n241\t                    .iter()\n242\t                    .filter_map(|v| serde_json::from_value(v.clone()).ok())\n243\t                    .collect();\n244\t                if !beads.is_empty() {\n245\t                    return Ok(beads);\n246\t                }\n247\t            }\n248\t        }\n249\t\n250\t        anyhow::bail!(\"failed to parse agent response as proposed beads\")\n251\t    }\n252\t\n253\t    /// Build the weave prompt from discovered docs and existing beads.\n254\t    ///\n255\t    /// Uses `config.prompt_template` when set; otherwise falls back to the\n256\t    /// built-in template. Template variables: `{doc_files}`, `{existing_beads}`,\n257\t    /// `{workspace}`.\n258\t    fn build_prompt(&self, doc_files: &str, existing_beads: &str) -> String {\n259\t        if let Some(template) = &self.config.prompt_template {\n260\t            return template\n261\t                .replace(\"{doc_files}\", doc_files)\n262\t                .replace(\"{existing_beads}\", existing_beads)\n263\t                .replace(\"{workspace}\", &self.workspace.display().to_string());\n264\t        }\n265\t\n266\t        // Built-in default template.\n267\t        format!(\n268\t            \"## Workspace Documentation\\n\\n\\\n269\t             {doc_files}\\n\\n\\\n270\t             ## Current Open Beads\\n\\n\\\n271\t             {existing_beads}\\n\\n\\\n272\t             ## Question\\n\\n\\\n273\t             Review the documentation above. Identify gaps where documented features, \\\n274\t             APIs, or workflows are incomplete, missing tests, or have no corresponding \\\n275\t             implementation bead.\\n\\n\\\n276\t             For each gap found, propose a bead with:\\n\\\n277\t             - title: concise description of what's missing\\n\\\n278\t             - body: what needs to be done to close the gap\\n\\\n279\t             - priority: 1 (critical), 2 (important), or 3 (nice-to-have)\\n\\n\\\n280\t             Output a JSON array of objects with \\\"title\\\", \\\"body\\\", and \\\"priority\\\" fields.\\n\\\n281\t             Do not propose beads that duplicate any existing open beads listed above.\\n\\\n282\t             If no gaps are found, respond with: NO_GAPS\"\n283\t        )\n284\t    }\n285\t}\n286\t\n287\t/// Extract a JSON block from markdown-fenced content.\n288\tfn extract_json_block(text: &str) -> Option<&str> {\n289\t    // Look for ```json ... ``` or ``` ... ```\n290\t    let start_markers = [\"```json\\n\", \"```json\\r\\n\", \"```\\n\", \"```\\r\\n\"];\n291\t    for marker in &start_markers {\n292\t        if let Some(start) = text.find(marker) {\n293\t            let content_start = start + marker.len();\n294\t            if let Some(end) = text[content_start..].find(\"```\") {\n295\t                return Some(&text[content_start..content_start + end]);\n296\t            }\n297\t        }\n298\t    }\n299\t    None\n300\t}\n301\t\n302\t/// Compute a short SHA-256 hash of a workspace path (for state filenames).\n303\tfn workspace_hash(workspace: &Path) -> String {\n304\t    let mut hasher = Sha256::new();\n305\t    hasher.update(workspace.display().to_string().as_bytes());\n306\t    let result = hasher.finalize();\n307\t    // Use first 16 hex chars for a short but unique filename.\n308\t    result\n309\t        .iter()\n310\t        .take(8)\n311\t        .fold(String::with_capacity(16), |mut acc, b| {\n312\t            use std::fmt::Write;\n313\t            let _ = write!(acc, \"{b:02x}\");\n314\t            acc\n315\t        })\n316\t}\n317\t\n318\t#[async_trait::async_trait]\n319\timpl super::Strand for WeaveStrand {\n320\t    fn name(&self) -> &str {\n321\t        \"weave\"\n322\t    }\n323\t\n324\t    async fn evaluate(&self, store: &dyn BeadStore) -> StrandResult {\n325\t        // Guard: disabled.\n326\t        if !self.config.enabled {\n327\t            tracing::debug!(\"weave strand disabled\");\n328\t            return StrandResult::NoWork;\n329\t        }\n330\t\n331\t        // Guard: workspace exclusion.\n332\t        if self.is_workspace_excluded() {\n333\t            tracing::debug!(\n334\t                workspace = %self.workspace.display(),\n335\t                \"weave strand: workspace excluded\"\n336\t            );\n337\t            return StrandResult::NoWork;\n338\t        }\n339\t\n340\t        // Guard: cooldown.\n341\t        let state_path = self.state_file_path();\n342\t        let mut state = match WeaveState::load(&state_path) {\n343\t            Ok(s) => s,\n344\t            Err(e) => {\n345\t                tracing::warn!(error = %e, \"failed to load weave state, using defaults\");\n346\t                WeaveState::default()\n347\t            }\n348\t        };\n349\t\n350\t        if !state.cooldown_elapsed(self.config.cooldown_hours) {\n351\t            tracing::debug!(\n352\t                last_run = ?state.last_run,\n353\t                cooldown_hours = self.config.cooldown_hours,\n354\t                \"weave strand: cooldown not elapsed\"\n355\t            );\n356\t            return StrandResult::NoWork;\n357\t        }\n358\t\n359\t        // Discover documentation files.\n360\t        let doc_files = self.discover_doc_files();\n361\t        if doc_files.is_empty() {\n362\t            tracing::debug!(\"weave strand: no documentation files found\");\n363\t            return StrandResult::NoWork;\n364\t        }\n365\t        let doc_content = Self::format_doc_files(&doc_files, &self.workspace);\n366\t\n367\t        // Query existing beads for dedup context.\n368\t        let existing_beads = match store.list_all().await {\n369\t            Ok(beads) => beads,\n370\t            Err(e) => {\n371\t                tracing::warn!(error = %e, \"weave strand: failed to list existing beads\");\n372\t                return StrandResult::Error(crate::types::StrandError::StoreError(\n373\t                    anyhow::anyhow!(e.to_string()),\n374\t                ));\n375\t            }\n376\t        };\n377\t        let existing_context = Self::format_existing_beads(&existing_beads);\n378\t\n379\t        // Build prompt and dispatch agent.\n380\t        let prompt = self.build_prompt(&doc_content, &existing_context);\n381\t        let response = match self.agent.analyze_gaps(&prompt, &self.workspace).await {\n382\t            Ok(r) => r,\n383\t            Err(e) => {\n384\t                tracing::warn!(error = %e, \"weave strand: agent dispatch failed\");\n385\t                return StrandResult::Error(crate::types::StrandError::StoreError(\n386\t                    anyhow::anyhow!(e.to_string()),\n387\t                ));\n388\t            }\n389\t        };\n390\t\n391\t        // Parse proposed beads.\n392\t        let proposed = match Self::parse_agent_response(&response) {\n393\t            Ok(p) => p,\n394\t            Err(e) => {\n395\t                tracing::warn!(error = %e, \"weave strand: failed to parse agent response\");\n396\t                // Update last_run even on parse failure to avoid rapid retries.\n397\t                state.last_run = Some(Utc::now());\n398\t                let _ = state.save(&state_path);\n399\t                return StrandResult::NoWork;\n400\t            }\n401\t        };\n402\t\n403\t        if proposed.is_empty() {\n404\t            tracing::info!(\"weave strand: agent found no gaps\");\n405\t            state.last_run = Some(Utc::now());\n406\t            let _ = state.save(&state_path);\n407\t            return StrandResult::NoWork;\n408\t        }\n409\t\n410\t        // Create beads (with guardrails).\n411\t        let mut created = 0u32;\n412\t        let existing_titles: HashSet<String> = existing_beads\n413\t            .iter()\n414\t            .map(|b| b.title.to_lowercase())\n415\t            .collect();\n416\t\n417\t        for proposed_bead in &proposed {\n418\t            // Guard: max beads per run.\n419\t            if created >= self.config.max_beads_per_run {\n420\t                tracing::info!(\n421\t                    max = self.config.max_beads_per_run,\n422\t                    \"weave strand: max beads per run reached\"\n423\t                );\n424\t                break;\n425\t            }\n426\t\n427\t            // Guard: dedup against seen titles.\n428\t            if state.is_duplicate(&proposed_bead.title) {\n429\t                tracing::debug!(\n430\t                    title = proposed_bead.title,\n431\t                    \"weave strand: skipping duplicate (seen before)\"\n432\t                );\n433\t                continue;\n434\t            }\n435\t\n436\t            // Guard: dedup against existing beads.\n437\t            if existing_titles.contains(&proposed_bead.title.to_lowercase()) {\n438\t                tracing::debug!(\n439\t                    title = proposed_bead.title,\n440\t                    \"weave strand: skipping duplicate (already exists)\"\n441\t                );\n442\t                state.mark_seen(&proposed_bead.title);\n443\t                continue;\n444\t            }\n445\t\n446\t            // Clamp priority to valid range.\n447\t            let priority = proposed_bead.priority.clamp(1, 3);\n448\t\n449\t            // Create the bead with weave-generated label.\n450\t            let body = format!(\n451\t                \"{}\\n\\n---\\nPriority: P{priority}\\nCreated by: weave strand\",\n452\t                proposed_bead.body\n453\t            );\n454\t            match store\n455\t                .create_bead(&proposed_bead.title, &body, &[\"weave-generated\"])\n456\t                .await\n457\t            {\n458\t                Ok(bead_id) => {\n459\t                    tracing::info!(\n460\t                        bead_id = bead_id.as_ref(),\n461\t                        title = proposed_bead.title,\n462\t                        \"weave strand: created bead\"\n463\t                    );\n464\t                    state.mark_seen(&proposed_bead.title);\n465\t                    created += 1;\n466\t                }\n467\t                Err(e) => {\n468\t                    tracing::warn!(\n469\t                        error = %e,\n470\t                        title = proposed_bead.title,\n471\t                        \"weave strand: failed to create bead\"\n472\t                    );\n473\t                }\n474\t            }\n475\t        }\n476\t\n477\t        // Update state.\n478\t        state.last_run = Some(Utc::now());\n479\t        if let Err(e) = state.save(&state_path) {\n480\t            tracing::warn!(error = %e, \"weave strand: failed to save state\");\n481\t        }\n482\t\n483\t        if created > 0 {\n484\t            tracing::info!(\n485\t                created,\n486\t                \"weave strand: created beads from documentation gaps\"\n487\t            );\n488\t            StrandResult::WorkCreated\n489\t        } else {\n490\t            tracing::info!(\"weave strand: no new beads created (all duplicates or filtered)\");\n491\t            StrandResult::NoWork\n492\t        }\n493\t    }\n494\t}\n495\t\n496\t// ─── CLI agent implementation ────────────────────────────────────────────────\n497\t\n498\t/// Production `WeaveAgent` that shells out to a CLI agent (e.g., `claude`).\n499\t///\n500\t/// The agent is invoked in `--print` mode so it emits its analysis as plain\n501\t/// text on stdout without tool-use side-effects. The prompt is written to a\n502\t/// temp file and fed via stdin redirection.\n503\tpub struct CliWeaveAgent {\n504\t    /// Agent binary name or path (e.g., `\"claude\"`).\n505\t    agent_cmd: String,\n506\t}\n507\t\n508\timpl CliWeaveAgent {\n509\t    /// Create a new `CliWeaveAgent`.\n510\t    ///\n511\t    /// `agent_cmd` is the binary used for analysis (typically taken from\n512\t    /// `config.agent.default`).\n513\t    pub fn new(agent_cmd: String) -> Self {\n514\t        CliWeaveAgent { agent_cmd }\n515\t    }\n516\t}\n517\t\n518\t#[async_trait::async_trait]\n519\timpl WeaveAgent for CliWeaveAgent {\n520\t    async fn analyze_gaps(&self, prompt: &str, workspace: &Path) -> Result<String> {\n521\t        // Write the prompt to a temp file.\n522\t        let tmp_dir = std::env::temp_dir().join(\"needle\");\n523\t        std::fs::create_dir_all(&tmp_dir).context(\"failed to create needle temp dir for weave\")?;\n524\t        let tmp_file = tmp_dir.join(format!(\"weave-{}.md\", std::process::id()));\n525\t        std::fs::write(&tmp_file, prompt).context(\"failed to write weave prompt to temp file\")?;\n526\t\n527\t        // Build the shell command: cd into workspace, pipe prompt to agent.\n528\t        let cmd = format!(\n529\t            \"cd {} && {} --print < {}\",\n530\t            workspace.display(),\n531\t            self.agent_cmd,\n532\t            tmp_file.display(),\n533\t        );\n534\t\n535\t        let output = tokio::process::Command::new(\"bash\")\n536\t            .arg(\"-c\")\n537\t            .arg(&cmd)\n538\t            .output()\n539\t            .await\n540\t            .with_context(|| format!(\"failed to spawn weave agent: {}\", self.agent_cmd))?;\n541\t\n542\t        // Always clean up the temp file.\n543\t        let _ = std::fs::remove_file(&tmp_file);\n544\t\n545\t        if !output.status.success() {\n546\t            anyhow::bail!(\n547\t                \"weave agent exited with code {}\",\n548\t                output.status.code().unwrap_or(-1)\n549\t            );\n550\t        }\n551\t\n552\t        Ok(String::from_utf8_lossy(&output.stdout).into_owned())\n553\t    }\n554\t}\n555\t\n556\t// ─── Unit tests ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n557\t\n558\t#[cfg(test)]\n559\tmod tests {\n560\t    use super::*;\n561\t    use }\n573\t\n574\t    impl MockAgent {\n575\t        fn new(response: &str) -> Self {\n576\t            MockAgent {\n577\t                response: Mutex::new(response.to_string()),\n578\t            }\n579\t        }\n580\t    }\n581\t\n582\t    #[async_trait::async_trait]\n583\t    impl WeaveAgent for MockAgent {\n584\t        async fn analyze_gaps(&self, _prompt: &str, _workspace: &Path) ->     }\n596\t    }\n597\t\n598\t    // ── Mock BeadStore ───────────────────────────────────────────────────\n599\t\n600\t    struct MockStore {\n601\t        beads: Vec<Bead>,\n602\t        created: Weave strand: gap analysis and bead creation from documentation.\n//!\n//! When all other strands (Pluck, Mend, Explore) returned NoWork,\n//! Weave analyzes workspace documentation for gaps and creates beads\n//! to address them.\n//!\n//! Heavily guardrailed (from v1 lessons):\n//! - **Opt-in only.** Disabled by default.\n//! - **Max beads per run.** Configurable, default 5.\n//! - **Cooldown.** Minimum hours between runs, default 24h.\n//! - **Dedup.** Tracks previously created titles to prevent duplicates.\n//! - **Workspace exclusion.** Configurable list of forbidden workspaces.\n//! - **Weave-generated label.** All created beads are labeled for filtering.\n\nuse std::collections::HashSet;\nuse std::path::{Path, PathBuf};\n\nuse anyhow::{Context, Result};\nuse chrono::{DateTime, Utc};\nuse serde::{Deserialize,
