────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\n/// Abstraction for agent invocation used by the Weave strand.\n///\n/// Production implementations wrap the `Dispatcher`; tests use mocks.\n#[async_trait::async_trait]\npub trait WeaveAgent: Send + Sync {\n    /// Invoke an agent with the given prompt, returning its raw text response.\n    async fn analyze_gaps(&self, prompt: &str, workspace: &Path) -> Result<String>;\n}\n\n// ─── Proposed bead (parsed from agent response) ──────────────────────────────\n\n/// A bead proposed by the agent during gap analysis.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub struct ProposedBead {\n    pub title: String,\n    pub body: String,\n    pub priority: u8,\n}\n\n// ─── Persistent state ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\n/// Persisted state for a workspace's weave runs.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Default, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub struct WeaveState {\n    /// Timestamp of the last weave run.\n    pub last_run: Option<DateTime<Utc>>,\n    /// Titles of beads previously created by weave (for dedup).\n    pub seen_titles: HashSet<String>,\n}\n\nimpl WeaveState {\n    /// Load state from disk, returning default if file doesn't exist.\n    fn load(path: &Path) -> Result<Self> {\n        match std::fs::read_to_string(path) {\n            Ok(data) => serde_json::from_str(&data)\n                .with_context(|| format!(\"failed to parse weave state: {}\", path.display())),\n            Err(e) if e.kind() == std::io::ErrorKind::NotFound => Ok(Self::default()),\n            Err(e) => {\n                Err(e).with_context(|| format!(\"failed to read weave state: {}\", path.display()))\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Persist state to disk.\n    fn save(&self, path: &Path) -> Result<()> {\n        if let Some(parent) = path.parent() {\n            std::fs::create_dir_all(parent)\n                .with_context(|| format!(\"failed to create state dir: {}\", parent.display()))?;\n        }\n        let data = serde_json::to_string_pretty(self).context(\"failed to serialize weave state\")?;\n        std::fs::write(path, data)\n            .with_context(|| format!(\"failed to write weave state: {}\", path.display()))\n    }\n\n    /// Check if cooldown has elapsed since last run.\n    fn cooldown_elapsed(&self, cooldown_hours: u64) -> bool {\n        match self.last_run {\n            None => true,\n            Some(last) => {\n                let elapsed = Utc::now().signed_duration_since(last);\n                elapsed.num_hours() >= cooldown_hours as i64\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Check if a title was already seen (dedup).\n    fn is_duplicate(&self, title: &str) -> bool {\n        self.seen_titles.contains(&title.to_lowercase())\n    }\n\n    /// Record a title as seen.\n    fn mark_seen(&mut self, title: &str) {\n        self.seen_titles.insert(title.to_lowercase());\n    }\n}\n\n// ─── WeaveStrand ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\n/// The Weave strand — analyzes documentation gaps and creates beads.\npub struct WeaveStrand {\n    config: WeaveConfig,\n    workspace: PathBuf,\n    state_dir: PathBuf,\n    agent: Box<dyn WeaveAgent>,\n}\n\nimpl WeaveStrand {\n    /// Create a new WeaveStrand.\n    ///\n    /// `state_dir` is the base directory for weave state files\n    /// (e.g., `~/.needle/state/weave/`).\n    pub fn new(\n        config: WeaveConfig,\n        workspace: PathBuf,\n        state_dir: PathBuf,\n        agent: Box<dyn WeaveAgent>,\n    ) -> Self {\n        WeaveStrand {\n            config,\n            workspace,\n            state_dir,\n            agent,\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Compute the state file path for a workspace.\n    ///\n    /// Uses a SHA-256 hash of the workspace path to create a unique filename.\n    fn state_file_path(&self) -> PathBuf {\n        let hash = workspace_hash(&self.workspace);\n        self.state_dir.join(format!(\"{hash}.json\"))\n    }\n\n    /// Check if this workspace is excluded from weave.\n    fn is_workspace_excluded(&self) -> bool {\n        self.config\n            .exclude_workspaces\n            .iter()\n            .any(|excluded| excluded == &self.workspace)\n    }\n\n    /// Discover documentation files in the workspace using configured patterns.\n    fn discover_doc_files(&self) -> Vec<PathBuf> {\n        let mut files = Vec::new();\n        for pattern in &self.config.doc_patterns {\n            let full_pattern = self.workspace.join(pattern).display().to_string();\n            if let Ok(entries) = glob::glob(&full_pattern) {\n                for entry in entries.flatten() {\n                    if entry.is_file() && !files.contains(&entry) {\n                        files.push(entry);\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n        files.sort();\n        files\n    }\n\n    /// Format documentation files into a string for the prompt.\n    fn format_doc_files(files: &[PathBuf], workspace: &Path) -> String {\n        if files.is_empty() {\n            return \"(no documentation files found)\".to_string();\n        }\n\n        let mut sections = Vec::new();\n        for file in files {\n            let rel_path = file\n                .strip_prefix(workspace)\n                .unwrap_or(file)\n                .display()\n                .to_string();\n            match std::fs::read_to_string(file) {\n                Ok(content) => {\n                    sections.push(format!(\"### {rel_path}\\n\\n{}\", content.trim_end()));\n                }\n                Err(_) => {\n                    sections.push(format!(\"### {rel_path}\\n\\n(failed to read)\"));\n                }\n            }\n        }\n        sections.join(\"\\n\\n\")\n    }\n\n    /// Format existing beads into a string for the prompt.\n    fn format_existing_beads(beads: &[crate::types::Bead]) -> String {\n        if beads.is_empty() {\n            return \"(no open beads)\".to_string();\n        }\n\n        beads\n            .iter()\n            .map(|b| {\n                let title = &b.title;\n                let id = b.id.as_ref();\n                let priority = b.priority;\n                format!(\"- [{id}] P{priority}: {title}\")\n            })\n            .collect::<Vec<_>>()\n            .join(\"\\n\")\n    }\n\n    /// Parse the agent response into proposed beads.\n    ///\n    /// The agent may return:\n    /// - `NO_GAPS` — no gaps found\n    /// - A JSON array of proposed beads\n    /// - A JSON object with a `beads` field containing an array\n    pub fn parse_agent_response(response: &str) -> Result<Vec<ProposedBead>> {\n        let trimmed = response.trim();\n\n        // Check for NO_GAPS sentinel.\n        if trimmed.contains(\"NO_GAPS\") {\n            return Ok(vec![]);\n        }\n\n        // Try parsing as a JSON array directly.\n        if let Ok(beads) = serde_json::from_str::<Vec<ProposedBead>>(trimmed) {\n            return Ok(beads);\n        }\n\n        // Try extracting JSON from markdown code fences.\n        let json_str = extract_json_block(trimmed).unwrap_or(trimmed);\n\n        // Try as array.\n        if let Ok(beads) = serde_json::from_str::<Vec<ProposedBead>>(json_str) {\n            return Ok(beads);\n        }\n\n        // Try as object with \"beads\" field.\n        if let Ok(obj) = serde_json::from_str::<serde_json::Value>(json_str) {\n            if let Some(arr) = obj.get(\"beads\").and_then(|v| v.as_array()) {\n                let beads: Vec<ProposedBead> = arr\n                    .iter()\n                    .filter_map(|v| serde_json::from_value(v.clone()).ok())\n                    .collect();\n                if !beads.is_empty() {\n                    return Ok(beads);\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        anyhow::bail!(\"failed to parse agent response as proposed beads\")\n    }\n\n    /// Build the weave prompt from discovered docs and existing beads.\n    ///\n    /// Uses `config.prompt_template` when set; otherwise falls back to the\n    /// built-in template. Template variables: `{doc_files}`, `{existing_beads}`,\n    /// `{workspace}`.\n    fn build_prompt(&self, doc_files: &str, existing_beads: &str) -> String {\n        if let Some(template) = &self.config.prompt_template {\n            return template\n                .replace(\"{doc_files}\", doc_files)\n                .replace(\"{existing_beads}\", existing_beads)\n                .replace(\"{workspace}\", &self.workspace.display().to_string());\n        }\n\n        // Built-in default template.\n        format!(\n            \"## Workspace Documentation\\n\\n\\\n             {doc_files}\\n\\n\\\n             ## Current Open Beads\\n\\n\\\n             {existing_beads}\\n\\n\\\n             ## Question\\n\\n\\\n             Review the documentation above. Identify gaps where documented features, \\\n             APIs, or workflows are incomplete, missing tests, or have no corresponding \\\n             implementation bead.\\n\\n\\\n             For each gap found, propose a bead with:\\n\\\n             - title: concise description of what's missing\\n\\\n             - body: what needs to be done to close the gap\\n\\\n             - priority: 1 (critical), 2 (important), or 3 (nice-to-have)\\n\\n\\\n             Output a JSON array of objects with \\\"title\\\", \\\"body\\\", and \\\"priority\\\" fields.\\n\\\n             Do not propose beads that duplicate any existing open beads listed above.\\n\\\n             If no gaps are found, respond with: NO_GAPS\"\n        )\n    }\n}\n\n/// Extract a JSON block from markdown-fenced content.\nfn extract_json_block(text: &str) -> Option<&str> {\n    // Look for ```json ... ``` or ``` ... ```\n    let start_markers = [\"```json\\n\", \"```json\\r\\n\", \"```\\n\", \"```\\r\\n\"];\n    for marker in &start_markers {\n        if let Some(start) = text.find(marker) {\n            let content_start = start + marker.len();\n            if let Some(end) = text[content_start..].find(\"```\") {\n                return Some(&text[content_start..content_start + end]);\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    None\n}\n\n/// Compute a short SHA-256 hash of a workspace path (for state filenames).\nfn workspace_hash(workspace: &Path) -> String {\n    let mut hasher = Sha256::new();\n    hasher.update(workspace.display().to_string().as_bytes());\n    let result = hasher.finalize();\n    // Use first 16 hex chars for a short but unique filename.\n    result\n        .iter()\n        .take(8)\n        .fold(String::with_capacity(16), |mut acc, b| {\n            use std::fmt::Write;\n            let _ = write!(acc, \"{b:02x}\");\n            acc\n        })\n}\n\n#[async_trait::async_trait]\nimpl super::Strand for WeaveStrand {\n    fn name(&self) -> &str {\n        \"weave\"\n    }\n\n    async fn evaluate(&self, store: &dyn BeadStore) -> StrandResult {\n        // Guard: disabled.\n        if !self.config.enabled {\n            tracing::debug!(\"weave strand disabled\");\n            return StrandResult::NoWork;\n        }\n\n        // Guard: workspace exclusion.\n        if self.is_workspace_excluded() {\n            tracing::debug!(\n                workspace = %self.workspace.display(),\n                \"weave strand: workspace excluded\"\n            );\n            return StrandResult::NoWork;\n        }\n\n        // Guard: cooldown.\n        let state_path = self.state_file_path();\n        let mut state = match WeaveState::load(&state_path) {\n            Ok(s) => s,\n            Err(e) => {\n                tracing::warn!(error = %e, \"failed to load weave state, using defaults\");\n                WeaveState::default()\n            }\n        };\n\n        if !state.cooldown_elapsed(self.config.cooldown_hours) {\n            tracing::debug!(\n                last_run = ?state.last_run,\n                cooldown_hours = self.config.cooldown_hours,\n                \"weave strand: cooldown not elapsed\"\n            );\n            return StrandResult::NoWork;\n        }\n\n        // Discover documentation files.\n        let doc_files = self.discover_doc_files();\n        if doc_files.is_empty() {\n            tracing::debug!(\"weave strand: no documentation files found\");\n            return StrandResult::NoWork;\n        }\n        let doc_content = Self::format_doc_files(&doc_files, &self.workspace);\n\n        // Query existing beads for dedup context.\n        let existing_beads = match store.list_all().await {\n            Ok(beads) => beads,\n            Err(e) => {\n                tracing::warn!(error = %e, \"weave strand: failed to list existing beads\");\n                return StrandResult::Error(crate::types::StrandError::StoreError(\n                    anyhow::anyhow!(e.to_string()),\n                ));\n            }\n        };\n        let existing_context = Self::format_existing_beads(&existing_beads);\n\n        // Build prompt and dispatch agent.\n        let prompt = self.build_prompt(&doc_content, &existing_context);\n        let response = match self.agent.analyze_gaps(&prompt, &self.workspace).await {\n            Ok(r) => r,\n            Err(e) => {\n                tracing::warn!(error = %e, \"weave strand: agent dispatch failed\");\n                return StrandResult::Error(crate::types::StrandError::StoreError(\n                    anyhow::anyhow!(e.to_string()),\n                ));\n            }\n        };\n\n        // Parse proposed beads.\n        let proposed = match Self::parse_agent_response(&response) {\n            Ok(p) => p,\n            Err(e) => {\n                tracing::warn!(error = %e, \"weave strand: failed to parse agent response\");\n                // Update last_run even on parse failure to avoid rapid retries.\n                state.last_run = Some(Utc::now());\n                let _ = state.save(&state_path);\n                return StrandResult::NoWork;\n            }\n        };\n\n        if proposed.is_empty() {\n            tracing::info!(\"weave strand: agent found no gaps\");\n            state.last_run = Some(Utc::now());\n            let _ = state.save(&state_path);\n            return StrandResult::NoWork;\n        }\n\n        // Create beads (with guardrails).\n        let mut created = 0u32;\n        let existing_titles: HashSet<String> = existing_beads\n            .iter()\n            .map(|b| b.title.to_lowercase())\n            .collect();\n\n        for proposed_bead in &proposed {\n            // Guard: max beads per run.\n            if created >= self.config.max_beads_per_run {\n                tracing::info!(\n                    max = self.config.max_beads_per_run,\n                    \"weave strand: max beads per run reached\"\n                );\n                break;\n            }\n\n            // Guard: dedup against seen titles.\n            if state.is_duplicate(&proposed_bead.title) {\n                tracing::debug!(\n                    title = proposed_bead.title,\n                    \"weave strand: skipping duplicate (seen before)\"\n                );\n                continue;\n            }\n\n            // Guard: dedup against existing beads.\n            if existing_titles.contains(&proposed_bead.title.to_lowercase()) {\n                tracing::debug!(\n                    title = proposed_bead.title,\n                    \"weave strand: skipping duplicate (already exists)\"\n                );\n                state.mark_seen(&proposed_bead.title);\n                continue;\n            }\n\n            // Clamp priority to valid range.\n            let priority = proposed_bead.priority.clamp(1, 3);\n\n            // Create the bead with weave-generated label.\n            let body = format!(\n                \"{}\\n\\n---\\nPriority: P{priority}\\nCreated by: weave strand\",\n                proposed_bead.body\n            );\n            match store\n                .create_bead(&proposed_bead.title, &body, &[\"weave-generated\"])\n                .await\n            {\n                Ok(bead_id) => {\n                    tracing::info!(\n                        bead_id = bead_id.as_ref(),\n                        title = proposed_bead.title,\n                        \"weave strand: created bead\"\n                    );\n                    state.mark_seen(&proposed_bead.title);\n                    created += 1;\n                }\n                Err(e) => {\n                    tracing::warn!(\n                        error = %e,\n                        title = proposed_bead.title,\n                        \"weave strand: failed to create bead\"\n                    );\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Update state.\n        state.last_run = Some(Utc::now());\n        if let Err(e) = state.save(&state_path) {\n            tracing::warn!(error = %e, \"weave strand: failed to save state\");\n        }\n\n        if created > 0 {\n            tracing::info!(\n                created,\n                \"weave strand: created beads from documentation gaps\"\n            );\n            StrandResult::WorkCreated\n        } else {\n            tracing::info!(\"weave strand: no new beads created (all duplicates or filtered)\");\n            StrandResult::NoWork\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n// ─── CLI agent implementation ────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\n/// Production `WeaveAgent` that shells out to a CLI agent (e.g., `claude`).\n///\n/// The agent is invoked in `--print` mode so it emits its analysis as plain\n/// text on stdout without tool-use side-effects. The prompt is written to a\n/// temp file and fed via stdin redirection.\npub struct CliWeaveAgent {\n    /// Agent binary name or path (e.g., `\"claude\"`).\n    agent_cmd: String,\n}\n\nimpl CliWeaveAgent {\n    /// Create a new `CliWeaveAgent`.\n    ///\n    /// `agent_cmd` is the binary used for analysis (typically taken from\n    /// `config.agent.default`).\n    pub fn new(agent_cmd: String) -> Self {\n        CliWeaveAgent { agent_cmd }\n    }\n}\n\n#[async_trait::async_trait]\nimpl WeaveAgent for CliWeaveAgent {\n    async fn analyze_gaps(&self, prompt: &str, workspace: &Path) -> Result<String> {\n        // Write the prompt to a temp file.\n        let tmp_dir = std::env::temp_dir().join(\"needle\");\n        std::fs::create_dir_all(&tmp_dir).context(\"failed to create needle temp dir for weave\")?;\n        let tmp_file = tmp_dir.join(format!(\"weave-{}.md\", std::process::id()));\n        std::fs::write(&tmp_file, prompt).context(\"failed to write weave prompt to temp file\")?;\n\n        // Build the shell command: cd into workspace, pipe prompt to agent.\n        let cmd = format!(\n            \"cd {} && {} --print < {}\",\n            workspace.display(),\n            self.agent_cmd,\n            tmp_file.display(),\n        );\n\n        let output = tokio::process::Command::new(\"bash\")\n            .arg(\"-c\")\n            .arg(&cmd)\n            .output()\n            .await\n            .with_context(|| format!(\"failed to spawn weave agent: {}\", self.agent_cmd))?;\n\n        // Always clean up the temp file.\n        let _ = std::fs::remove_file(&tmp_file);\n\n        if !output.status.success() {\n            anyhow::bail!(\n                \"weave agent exited with code {}\",\n                output.status.code().unwrap_or(-1)\n            );\n        }\n\n        Ok(String::from_utf8_lossy(&output.stdout).into_owned())\n    }\n}\n\n// ─── Unit tests ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\n#[cfg(test)]\nmod tests {\n    use super::*;\n    use crate::bead_store::{Filters, RepairReport};\n    use crate::types::{Bead, BeadId, BeadStatus, ClaimResult};\n\n    use anyhow::Result;\n    use chrono::{TimeZone, Utc};\n    use std::sync::Mutex;\n\n    // ── Mock WeaveAgent ──────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\n    struct MockAgent {\n        response: Mutex<String>,\n    }\n\n    impl MockAgent {\n        fn new(response: &str) -> Self {\n            MockAgent {\n                response: Mutex::new(response.to_string()),\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    #[async_trait::async_trait]\n    impl WeaveAgent for MockAgent {\n        async fn analyze_gaps(&self, _prompt: &str, _workspace: &Path) -> Result<String> {\n            Ok(self.response.lock().unwrap().clone())\n        }\n    }\n\n    struct FailingAgent;\n\n    #[async_trait::async_trait]\n    impl WeaveAgent for FailingAgent {\n        async fn analyze_gaps(&self, _prompt: &str, _workspace: &Path) -> Result<String> {\n            anyhow::bail!(\"agent dispatch failed\")\n        }\n    }\n\n    // ── Mock BeadStore ───────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\n    struct MockStore {\n        beads: Vec<Bead>,\n        created: Mutex<Vec<(String, String, Vec<String>)>>,\n    }\n\n    impl MockStore {\n        fn new(beads: Vec<Bead>) -> Self {\n            MockStore {\n                beads,\n                created: Mutex::new(Vec::new()),\n            }\n        }\n\n        fn empty() -> Self {\n            Self::new(vec![])\n        }\n\n        fn created_beads(&self) -> Vec<(String, String, Vec<String>)> {\n            self.created.lock().unwrap().clone()\n        }\n    }\n\n    #[async_trait::async_trait]\n    impl BeadStore for MockStore {\n        async fn list_all(&self) -> Result<Vec<Bead>> {\n            Ok(self.beads.clone())\n        }\n        async fn ready(&self, _filters: &Filters) -> Result<Vec<Bead>> {\n            Ok(self.beads.clone())\n        }\n        async fn show(&self, _id: &BeadId) -> Result<Bead> {\n            anyhow::bail!(\"not implemented\")\n        }\n        async fn claim(&self, _id: &BeadId, _actor: &str) -> Result<ClaimResult> {\n            anyhow::bail!(\"not implemented\")\n        }\n        async fn release(&self, _id: &BeadId) -> Result<()> {\n            Ok(())\n        }\n        async fn reopen(&self, _id: &BeadId) -> Result<()> {\n            Ok(())\n        }\n        async fn labels(&self, _id: &BeadId) -> Result<Vec<String>> {\n            Ok(vec![])\n        }\n        async fn add_label(&self, _id: &BeadId, _label: &str) -> Result<()> {\n            Ok(())\n        }\n        async fn remove_label(&self, _id: &BeadId, _label: &str) -> Result<()> {\n            Ok(())\n        }\n        async fn create_bead(&self, title: &str, body: &str, labels: &[&str]) -> Result<BeadId> {\n            self.created.lock().unwrap().push((\n                title.to_string(),\n                body.to_string(),\n                labels.iter().map(|s| s.to_string()).collect(),\n            ));\n            Ok(BeadId::from(format!(\"weave-{}\", title.len())))\n        }\n        async fn doctor_repair(&self) -> Result<RepairReport> {\n            Ok(RepairReport::default())\n        }\n        async fn doctor_check(&self) -> Result<RepairReport> {\n            Ok(RepairReport::default())\n        }\n        async fn full_rebuild(&self) -> Result<()> {\n            Ok(())\n        }\n        async fn add_dependency(&self, _blocker_id: &BeadId, _blocked_id: &BeadId) -> Result<()> {\n            Ok(())\n        }\n    }\n\n    // ── Helpers ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\n    fn make_bead(id: &str, title: &str) -> Bead {\n        let dt = Utc.with_ymd_and_hms(2026, 1, 1, 0, 0, 0).unwrap();\n        Bead {\n            id: BeadId::from(id.to_string()),\n            title: title.to_string(),\n            body: None,\n            priority: 1,\n            status: BeadStatus::Open,\n            assignee: None,\n            labels: vec![],\n            workspace: PathBuf::from(\"/tmp/test\"),\n            dependencies: vec![],\n            dependents: vec![],\n            created_at: dt,\n            updated_at: dt,\n        }\n    }\n\n    fn make_test_workspace() -> (tempfile::TempDir, PathBuf) {\n        let dir = tempfile::tempdir().unwrap();\n        let workspace = dir.path().to_path_buf();\n        // Create a documentation file.\n        std::fs::write(\n            workspace.join(\"README.md\"),\n            \"# Test Project\\n\\nA test project.\",\n        )\n        .unwrap();\n        (dir, workspace)\n    }\n\n    fn make_enabled_config() -> WeaveConfig {\n        WeaveConfig {\n            enabled: true,\n            max_beads_per_run: 5,\n            cooldown_hours: 24,\n            exclude_workspaces: vec![],\n            doc_patterns: vec![\"README*\".to_string()],\n            prompt_template: None,\n        }\n    }\n\n    use super::super::Strand;\n\n    // ── Tests ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\n    #[test]\n    fn strand_name_is_weave() {\n        let dir = tempfile::tempdir().unwrap();\n        let strand = WeaveStrand::new(\n            WeaveConfig::default(),\n            PathBuf::from(\"/tmp\"),\n            dir.path().to_path_buf(),\n            Box::new(MockAgent::new(\"NO_GAPS\")),\n        );\n        assert_eq!(strand.name(), \"weave\");\n    }\n\n    #[tokio::test]\n    async fn disabled_returns_no_work() {\n        let dir = tempfile::tempdir().unwrap();\n        let strand = WeaveStrand::new(\n            WeaveConfig::default(), // disabled by default\n            PathBuf::from(\"/tmp\"),\n            dir.path().to_path_buf(),\n            Box::new(MockAgent::new(\"NO_GAPS\")),\n        );\n        let store = MockStore::empty();\n        let result = strand.evaluate(&store).await;\n        assert!(matches!(result, StrandResult::NoWork));\n    }\n\n    #[tokio::test]\n    async fn excluded_workspace_returns_no_work() {\n        let (_dir, workspace) = make_test_workspace();\n        let state_dir = tempfile::tempdir().unwrap();\n        let config = WeaveConfig {\n            enabled: true,\n            exclude_workspaces: vec![workspace.clone()],\n            ..WeaveConfig::default()\n        };\n        let strand = WeaveStrand::new(\n            config,\n            workspace,\n            state_dir.path().to_path_buf(),\n            Box::new(MockAgent::new(\"NO_GAPS\")),\n        );\n        let store = MockStore::empty();\n        let result = strand.evaluate(&store).await;\n        assert!(matches!(result, StrandResult::NoWork));\n    }\n\n    #[tokio::test]\n    async fn cooldown_not_elapsed_returns_no_work() {\n        let (_dir, workspace) = make_test_workspace();\n        let state_dir = tempfile::tempdir().unwrap();\n\n        // Write state with recent last_run.\n        let state = WeaveState {\n            last_run: Some(Utc::now()),\n            seen_titles: Reflect strand: meta-analysis and learning consolidation.\n//!\n//! Strand 7 in the waterfall. Runs after all other strands return NoWork.\n//! This is the last productive strategy before giving up — meta-analysis\n//! only runs when there is genuinely nothing else to do.\n//!\n//! KAIROS-inspired four-phase cycle:\n//! 1. **Orient** — read current learnings.md and existing skills, check sizes.\n//! 2. **Gather** — read bead close bodies from issues.jsonl since last\n//!    consolidation; read traces for failed beads.\n//! 3. **Consolidate** — extract retrospective blocks, identify cross-bead\n//!    patterns, merge into learnings.md, deduplicate, resolve contradictions.\n//!    Promote learnings with reinforcement_count ≥ 3 to skill files.\n//! 4. **Prune** — remove entries older than `learning_retention_days` days\n//!    without reinforcement, compress similar entries, enforce `max_learnings`.\n//!\n//! Entry conditions (checked before running):\n//! - `strands.reflect.enabled` is true\n//! - 10+ beads closed since last consolidation (configurable)\n//! - 24+ hours since last consolidation (configurable cooldown)\n//!\n//! Guardrails:\n//! - Max `max_learnings_per_run` new learnings added per run\n//! - Max `max_skills_per_run` skill files created/updated per run\n//! - CLAUDE.md is read-only — never written\n//!\n//! Depends on: `config`, `learning`, `telemetry`, `types`.\n\nuse std::path::{Path, PathBuf};\n\nuse anyhow::{Context, Result};\nuse chrono::{DateTime, Utc};\nuse serde::{Deserialize, Serialize};\n\nuse crate::bead_store::BeadStore;\nuse crate::config::ReflectConfig;\nuse crate::learning::{\n    BeadType, Confidence, GlobalLearningsFile, LearningEntry, LearningsFile, Retrospective,\n};\nuse crate::skill::{render_skill_file, SkillFrontmatter, SkillLibrary};\nuse crate::telemetry::{EventKind, Telemetry};\nuse crate::types::{StrandError, StrandResult};\n\n// ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n// State persistence\n// ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\n/// Persisted state for the Reflect strand.\n#[derive(Debug, Serialize, Deserialize)]\nstruct ReflectState {\n    /// Timestamp of the last successful consolidation.\n    last_consolidation: DateTime<Utc>,\n    /// Total closed beads at the time of last consolidation.\n    beads_at_last_consolidation: u64,\n}\n\nimpl ReflectState {\n    fn load(state_dir: &Path) -> Result<Option<Self>> {\n        let path = state_dir.join(\"reflect_state.json\");\n        if !path.exists() {\n            return Ok(None);\n        }\n        let content = std::fs::read_to_string(&path)\n            .with_context(|| format!(\"failed to read reflect state: {}\", path.display()))?;\n        let state: ReflectState =\n            serde_json::from_str(&content).with_context(|| \"failed to parse reflect state\")?;\n        Ok(Some(state))\n    }\n\n    fn save(&self, state_dir: &Path) -> Result<()> {\n        std::fs::create_dir_all(state_dir)\n            .with_context(|| format!(\"failed to create state dir: {}\", state_dir.display()))?;\n        let path = state_dir.join(\"reflect_state.json\");\n        let content = serde_json::to_string_pretty(self)?;\n        std::fs::write(&path, content)\n            .with_context(|| format!(\"failed to write reflect state: {}\", path.display()))?;\n        Ok(())\n    }\n}\n\n// ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n// Bead record (minimal, parsed from issues.jsonl)\n// ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\n/// Minimal closed-bead record read from issues.jsonl.\n#[derive(Debug, Deserialize)]\nstruct ClosedBeadRecord {\n    id: String,\n    status: String,\n    close_reason: Option<String>,\n    closed_at: Option<DateTime<Utc>>,\n    assignee: Option<String>,\n    #[serde(default)]\n    labels: Vec<String>,\n}\n\n// ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n// Summary\n// ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\n/// Work performed during one Reflect cycle.\n#[derive(Debug, Default)]\npub struct ReflectSummary {\n    pub beads_processed: usize,\n    pub learnings_added: usize,\n    pub learnings_pruned: usize,\n    pub skills_promoted: usize,\n    /// Number of learnings promoted to the global learnings file.\n    pub global_learnings_promoted: usize,\n}\n\n// ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n// Strand\n// ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\n/// The Reflect strand — meta-analysis and learning consolidation.\npub struct ReflectStrand {\n    config: ReflectConfig,\n    workspace: PathBuf,\n    state_dir: PathBuf,\n    telemetry: Telemetry,\n    /// Other workspaces to scan for cross-workspace patterns.\n    known_workspaces: Vec<PathBuf>,\n    /// Path to the global learnings file.\n    global_learnings_path: PathBuf,\n    /// Maximum entries in the global learnings file.\n    max_global_learnings: usize,\n}\n\nimpl ReflectStrand {\n    /// Create a new ReflectStrand.\n    ///\n    /// - `config`: reflect strand configuration\n    /// - `workspace`: workspace root (where `.beads/` lives)\n    /// - `state_dir`: directory for persisting reflect state (`~/.needle/state/reflect/`)\n    /// - `telemetry`: telemetry emitter\n    pub fn new(\n        config: ReflectConfig,\n        workspace: PathBuf,\n        state_dir: PathBuf,\n        telemetry: Telemetry,\n    ) -> Self {\n        ReflectStrand {\n            config,\n            workspace,\n            state_dir,\n            telemetry,\n            known_workspaces: Vec::new(),\n            global_learnings_path: PathBuf::new(),\n            max_global_learnings: 40,\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Configure cross-workspace detection and global learnings promotion.\n    ///\n    /// - `known_workspaces`: other workspace paths to check for matching patterns\n    /// - `global_learnings_path`: path to `~/.config/needle/global-learnings.md`\n    /// - `max_global_learnings`: cap on total entries in the global file (default: 40)\n    pub fn with_global(\n        mut self,\n        known_workspaces: Vec<PathBuf>,\n        global_learnings_path: PathBuf,\n        max_global_learnings: usize,\n    ) -> Self {\n        self.known_workspaces = known_workspaces;\n        self.global_learnings_path = global_learnings_path;\n        self.max_global_learnings = max_global_learnings;\n        self\n    }\n\n    /// Run the four-phase consolidation cycle.\n    ///\n    /// `force` bypasses cooldown and minimum bead threshold checks (used by\n    /// the `needle reflect` CLI command).\n    pub fn consolidate(&self, force: bool) -> Result<ReflectSummary> {\n        // ── Phase 1: Orient ───────────────────────────────────────────────────\n        let state = ReflectState::load(&self.state_dir)?;\n\n        let issues_path = self.workspace.join(\".beads\").join(\"issues.jsonl\");\n        if !issues_path.exists() {\n            tracing::debug!(\"reflect: no issues.jsonl found, skipping\");\n            return Ok(ReflectSummary::default());\n        }\n\n        // Count total closed beads and collect those since last consolidation.\n        let all_closed = self.read_closed_beads(&issues_path)?;\n        let total_closed = all_closed.len() as u64;\n\n        let since_last: Vec<&ClosedBeadRecord> = match &state {\n            Some(s) => all_closed\n                .iter()\n                .filter(|b| {\n                    b.closed_at\n                        .map(|t| t > s.last_consolidation)\n                        .unwrap_or(false)\n                })\n                .collect(),\n            None => all_closed.iter().collect(),\n        };\n\n        let beads_since = since_last.len();\n\n        if !force {\n            // Check minimum bead threshold.\n            if beads_since < self.config.min_beads_since_last {\n                tracing::debug!(\n                    beads_since,\n                    threshold = self.config.min_beads_since_last,\n                    \"reflect: below minimum bead threshold, skipping\"\n                );\n                let _ = self.telemetry.emit(EventKind::ReflectSkipped {\n                    reason: format!(\n                        \"only {} beads closed since last consolidation (need {})\",\n                        beads_since, self.config.min_beads_since_last\n                    ),\n                });\n                return Ok(ReflectSummary::default());\n            }\n\n            // Check cooldown.\n            if let Some(s) = &state {\n                let hours_since = (Utc::now() - s.last_consolidation).num_hours() as u64;\n                if hours_since < self.config.cooldown_hours {\n                    tracing::debug!(\n                        hours_since,\n                        cooldown = self.config.cooldown_hours,\n                        \"reflect: cooldown not elapsed, skipping\"\n                    );\n                    let _ = self.telemetry.emit(EventKind::ReflectSkipped {\n                        reason: format!(\n                            \"cooldown not elapsed ({}/{}h)\",\n                            hours_since, self.config.cooldown_hours\n                        ),\n                    });\n                    return Ok(ReflectSummary::default());\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        let _ = self.telemetry.emit(EventKind::ReflectStarted {\n            beads_since_last: beads_since,\n        });\n\n        tracing::info!(beads_since, force, \"reflect: starting consolidation cycle\");\n\n        // ── Phase 2: Gather ───────────────────────────────────────────────────\n        let mut retro_entries: Vec<(String, Retrospective)> = Vec::new();\n\n        for bead in &since_last {\n            if let Some(reason) = &bead.close_reason {\n                match Retrospective::parse_from_close_body(reason) {\n                    Ok(Some(retro)) if retro.is_meaningful() => {\n                        retro_entries.push((bead.id.clone(), retro));\n                    }\n                    Ok(_) => {}\n                    Err(e) => {\n                        tracing::warn!(bead_id = %bead.id, error = %e, \"failed to parse retrospective\");\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        tracing::debug!(\n            retro_count = retro_entries.len(),\n            \"reflect: gathered retrospectives\"\n        );\n\n        // ── Phase 3: Consolidate ──────────────────────────────────────────────\n        let mut learnings = LearningsFile::load(&self.workspace)?;\n        let mut summary = ReflectSummary {\n            beads_processed: beads_since,\n            ..Default::default()\n        };\n\n        // Extract learning entries from retrospectives.\n        let mut candidate_entries: Vec<LearningEntry> = Vec::new();\n\n        for (bead_id, retro) in &retro_entries {\n            // Determine bead type from labels if available.\n            let bead_type = self.infer_bead_type_from_id(bead_id, &all_closed);\n            let worker = self.infer_worker_from_id(bead_id, &all_closed);\n\n            if let Some(text) = &retro.reusable_pattern {\n                candidate_entries.push(LearningEntry::new(\n                    bead_id.clone(),\n                    worker.clone(),\n                    bead_type.clone(),\n                    text.clone(),\n                    Confidence::High,\n                    format!(\"reusable-pattern from {bead_id}\"),\n                ));\n            }\n            if let Some(text) = &retro.what_worked {\n                candidate_entries.push(LearningEntry::new(\n                    bead_id.clone(),\n                    worker.clone(),\n                    bead_type.clone(),\n                    text.clone(),\n                    Confidence::Medium,\n                    format!(\"what-worked from {bead_id}\"),\n                ));\n            }\n            if let Some(text) = &retro.surprise {\n                candidate_entries.push(LearningEntry::new(\n                    bead_id.clone(),\n                    worker.clone(),\n                    bead_type.clone(),\n                    text.clone(),\n                    Confidence::Medium,\n                    format!(\"surprise from {bead_id}\"),\n                ));\n            }\n            if let Some(text) = &retro.what_didnt {\n                candidate_entries.push(LearningEntry::new(\n                    bead_id.clone(),\n                    worker.clone(),\n                    bead_type.clone(),\n                    text.clone(),\n                    Confidence::Low,\n                    format!(\"what-didnt-work from {bead_id}\"),\n                ));\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Reinforce existing entries that match any closed bead ID, then add\n        // non-duplicate candidates up to max_learnings_per_run.\n        for bead in &since_last {\n            let _ = learnings.reinforce_entry(&bead.id);\n        }\n\n        let mut added = 0usize;\n        for candidate in candidate_entries {\n            if added >= self.config.max_learnings_per_run {\n                break;\n            }\n            // Skip if a similar entry already exists (dedup).\n            let similar = learnings.find_similar(&candidate.observation);\n            if !similar.is_empty() {\n                // Reinforce the most similar entry instead of adding a duplicate.\n                let most_similar_id = similar[0].bead_id.clone();\n                let _ = learnings.reinforce_entry(&most_similar_id);\n                continue;\n            }\n            learnings.add_entry(candidate)?;\n            added += 1;\n        }\n        summary.learnings_added = added;\n\n        // Promote high-reinforcement entries to skill files.\n        let promoted = self.promote_to_skills(learnings.entries())?;\n        summary.skills_promoted = promoted;\n\n        // Promote cross-workspace patterns to global learnings.\n        let global_promoted = self.promote_cross_workspace_patterns(&learnings)?;\n        summary.global_learnings_promoted = global_promoted;\n\n        // ── Phase 4: Prune ────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n        let pruned = learnings.prune_stale()?;\n        summary.learnings_pruned = pruned;\n\n        // Enforce max_learnings cap.\n        let over_limit = learnings.consolidate(self.config.max_learnings)?;\n        summary.learnings_pruned += over_limit;\n\n        // Persist updated state.\n        let new_state = ReflectState {\n            last_consolidation: Utc::now(),\n            beads_at_last_consolidation: total_closed,\n        };\n        new_state.save(&self.state_dir)?;\n\n        let _ = self.telemetry.emit(EventKind::ReflectConsolidated {\n            learnings_added: summary.learnings_added,\n            learnings_pruned: summary.learnings_pruned,\n            skills_promoted: summary.skills_promoted,\n            beads_processed: summary.beads_processed,\n        });\n\n        tracing::info!(\n            learnings_added = summary.learnings_added,\n            learnings_pruned = summary.learnings_pruned,\n            skills_promoted = summary.skills_promoted,\n            beads_processed = summary.beads_processed,\n            \"reflect: consolidation complete\"\n        );\n\n        Ok(summary)\n    }\n\n    // ── Helpers ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\n    /// Read all closed beads from issues.jsonl.\n    fn read_closed_beads(&self, issues_path: &Path) -> Result<Vec<ClosedBeadRecord>> {\n        let content = std::fs::read_to_string(issues_path)\n            .with_context(|| format!(\"failed to read {}\", issues_path.display()))?;\n\n        let mut beads = Vec::new();\n        for (line_no, line) in content.lines().enumerate() {\n            let line = line.trim();\n            if line.is_empty() {\n                continue;\n            }\n            match serde_json::from_str::<ClosedBeadRecord>(line) {\n                Ok(record) if record.status == \"closed\" => beads.push(record),\n                Ok(_) => {}\n                Err(e) => {\n                    tracing::warn!(line = line_no + 1, error = %e, \"reflect: failed to parse issues.jsonl line\");\n                }\n            }\n        }\n        Ok(beads)\n    }\n\n    /// Infer bead type from labels in the closed bead record.\n    fn infer_bead_type_from_id(&self, bead_id: &str, all_closed: &[ClosedBeadRecord]) -> BeadType {\n        let record = all_closed.iter().find(|b| b.id == bead_id);\n        if let Some(rec) = record {\n            for label in &rec.labels {\n                if let Some(bt) = BeadType::from_str(label) {\n                    return bt;\n                }\n            }\n        }\n        BeadType::Other\n    }\n\n    /// Infer worker from the assignee field of the closed bead record.\n    fn infer_worker_from_id(&self, bead_id: &str, all_closed: &[ClosedBeadRecord]) -> String {\n        all_closed\n            .iter()\n            .find(|b| b.id == bead_id)\n            .and_then(|b| b.assignee.clone())\n            .unwrap_or_else(|| \"unknown\".to_string())\n    }\n\n    /// Promote learning entries with reinforcement_count >= 3 to skill files.\n    ///\n    /// Creates `.beads/skills/<slug>.md` for each promoted entry.\n    /// Returns the number of skills created this run.\n    fn promote_to_skills(&self, entries: &[LearningEntry]) -> Result<usize> {\n        let skills_dir = self.workspace.join(\".beads\").join(\"skills\");\n        let mut promoted = 0usize;\n\n        // Build set of already-promoted bead IDs to avoid re-promoting.\n        let already_promoted = self.read_promoted_ids(&skills_dir);\n\n        for entry in entries {\n            if promoted >= self.config.max_skills_per_run {\n                break;\n            }\n            if entry.reinforcement_count < 3 {\n                continue;\n            }\n            if already_promoted.contains(&entry.bead_id) {\n                continue;\n            }\n\n            match self.write_skill_file(&skills_dir, entry) {\n                Ok(()) => promoted += 1,\n                Err(e) => {\n                    tracing::warn!(bead_id = %entry.bead_id, error = %e, \"reflect: failed to write skill file\");\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        Ok(promoted)\n    }\n\n    /// Read the set of bead IDs that have already been promoted to skills.\n    fn read_promoted_ids(&self, _skills_dir: &Path) -> std::collections::HashSet<String> {\n        match SkillLibrary::load(&self.workspace) {\n            Ok(lib) => lib.promoted_source_beads(),\n            Err(e) => {\n                tracing::warn!(error = %e, \"reflect: failed to load skill library for promoted IDs\");\n                std::collections::HashSet::new()\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Scan known workspaces for learnings that match entries in the current workspace,\n    /// promoting matches (cross-workspace patterns) to the global learnings file.\n    ///\n    /// An entry is promoted when a similar observation appears in at least one other\n    /// known workspace. Returns the number of entries promoted this run.\n    fn promote_cross_workspace_patterns(&self, learnings: &LearningsFile) -> Result<usize> {\n        // Skip when not configured.\n        if self.global_learnings_path.as_os_str().is_empty() || self.known_workspaces.is_empty() {\n            return Ok(0);\n        }\n\n        let mut global = GlobalLearningsFile::load(&self.global_learnings_path)?;\n\n        // Load learnings files for all known workspaces, skipping failures.\n        let mut other_learnings: Vec<LearningsFile> = Vec::new();\n        for ws in &self.known_workspaces {\n            match LearningsFile::load(ws) {\n                Ok(lf) if !lf.entries().is_empty() => other_learnings.push(lf),\n                Ok(_) => {}\n                Err(e) => {\n                    tracing::warn!(\n                        workspace = %ws.display(),\n                        error = %e,\n                        \"reflect: failed to load learnings for cross-workspace scan\"\n                    );\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        if other_learnings.is_empty() {\n            return Ok(0);\n        }\n\n        let mut promoted = 0usize;\n\n        for entry in learnings.entries() {\n            // Check if any other workspace has a similar observation.\n            let appears_in_other = other_learnings\n                .iter()\n                .any(|other| !other.find_similar(&entry.observation).is_empty());\n\n            if !appears_in_other {\n                continue;\n            }\n\n            if global.promote(entry.clone(), self.max_global_learnings) {\n                promoted += 1;\n                tracing::info!(\n                    bead_id = %entry.bead_id,\n                    observation = %entry.observation,\n                    \"reflect: promoted cross-workspace learning to global\"\n                );\n            }\n        }\n\n        if promoted > 0 {\n            global.write()?;\n        }\n\n        Ok(promoted)\n    }\n\n    /// Write a skill file for a promoted learning entry (YAML frontmatter format).\n    fn write_skill_file(&self, skills_dir: &Path, entry: &LearningEntry) -> Result<()> {\n        std::fs::create_dir_all(skills_dir)\n            .with_context(|| format!(\"failed to create skills dir: {}\", skills_dir.display()))?;\n\n        let slug = slugify(&entry.observation);\n        let filename = format!(\"{}-{}.md\", &slug[..slug.len().min(40)], &entry.bead_id);\n        let path = skills_dir.join(&filename);\n\n        let frontmatter = SkillFrontmatter {\n            task_types: vec![entry.bead_type.as_str().to_string()],\n            labels: vec![],\n            success_count: 0,\n            last_used: None,\n            source_beads: vec![entry.bead_id.clone()],\n        };\n\n        let body = format!(\n            \"## {}\\n\\n{}\\n\\n**Worker:** {}\\n**Source:** {}\\n\",\n            truncate(&entry.observation, 60),\n            entry.observation,\n            entry.worker,\n            entry.source,\n        );\n\n        let content = render_skill_file(&frontmatter, &body)\n            .with_context(|| format!(\"failed to render skill file: {filename}\"))?;\n\n        std::fs::write(&path, content)\n            .with_context(|| format!(\"failed to write skill file: {}\", path.display()))?;\n\n        tracing::info!(\n            bead_id = %entry.bead_id,\n            file = %filename,\n            reinforcement_count = entry.reinforcement_count,\n            \"reflect: promoted learning to skill file\"\n        );\n        Ok(())\n    }\n}\n\n#[async_trait::async_trait]\nimpl super::Strand for ReflectStrand {\n    fn name(&self) -> &str {\n        \"reflect\"\n    }\n\n    async fn evaluate(&self, _store: &dyn BeadStore) -> StrandResult {\n        if !self.config.enabled {\n            return StrandResult::NoWork;\n        }\n\n        match self.consolidate(false) {\n            Ok(_) => StrandResult::NoWork,\n            Err(e) => StrandResult::Error(StrandError::ConfigError(format!(\n                \"reflect consolidation failed: {e}\"\n            ))),\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n// ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n// Utilities\n// ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\n/// Create a URL-safe slug from a string.\nfn slugify(s: &str) -> String {\n    s.to_lowercase()\n        .chars()\n        .map(|c| if c.is_alphanumeric() { c } else { '-' })\n        .collect::<String>()\n        .split('-')\n        .filter(|s| !s.is_empty())\n        .collect::<Vec<_>>()\n        .join(\"-\")\n}\n\n/// Truncate a string to at most `max_chars` characters.\nfn truncate(s: &str, max_chars: usize) -> &str {\n    if s.len() <= max_chars {\n        s\n    } else {\n        &s[..max_chars]\n    }\n}\n\n// ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n// Tests\n// ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\n#[cfg(test)]\nmod tests {\n    use super::*;\n    use crate::strand::Strand as _;\n\n    #[test]\n    fn slugify_basic() {\n        assert_eq!(slugify(\"Hello World!\"), \"hello-world\");\n        assert_eq!(slugify(\"foo_bar baz\"), \"foo-bar-baz\");\n        assert_eq!(slugify(\"multiple---dashes\"), \"multiple-dashes\");\n    }\n\n    #[test]\n    fn truncate_short() {\n        assert_eq!(truncate(\"hello\", 10), \"hello\");\n    }\n\n    #[test]\n    fn truncate_exact() {\n        assert_eq!(truncate(\"hello\", 5), \"hello\");\n    }\n\n    #[test]\n    fn truncate_long() {\n        assert_eq!(truncate(\"hello world\", 5), \"hello\");\n    }\n\n    #[test]\n    fn     PathBuf::from(\"/tmp\"),\n            PathBuf::from(\"/tmp/state\"),\n            tel,\n        );\n        assert_eq!(strand.name(), \"reflect\");\n    }\n\n    #[tokio::test]\n    async fn assert_eq!(loaded.beads_at_last_consolidation, 42);\n    }\n\n    fn make_strand_with_global(\n        workspace: &std::path::Path,\n        known_workspaces: Vec<std::path::PathBuf>,\n        global_path: std::path::PathBuf,\n        max_global: usize,\n    ) -> ReflectStrand {\n        let config = ReflectConfig {\n            enabled: true,\n            min_beads_since_last: 100,\n            cooldown_hours: 9999,\n            ..Default::default()\n        };\n        let tel = Telemetry::new(\"test\".to_string());\n        ReflectStrand::new(\n            config,\n            workspace.to_path_buf(),\n            workspace.join(\"state\"),\n            tel,\n        )\n        .with_global(known_workspaces, global_path, max_global)\n    }\n\n    fn write_learnings(workspace: &std::path::Path, entries: &[(&str, &str)]) {\n        // entries: (bead_id, observation)\n        let beads_dir = workspace.join(\".beads\");\n        std::fs::create_dir_all(&beads_dir).unwrap();\n        let mut content = String::from(\"# Workspace Learnings\\n\\n\");\n        for (bead_id, observation) in entries {\n            content.push_str(&format!(\n                \"### 2026-04-04 | bead: {} | worker: alpha | type: other | reinforced: 0\\n\\\n                 - **Observation:** {}\\n\\\n                 - **Confidence:** high\\n\\\n                 - **Source:** test\\n\\n\",\n                bead_id, observation\n            ));\n        }\n        std::fs::write(beads_dir.join(\"learnings.md\"), content).unwrap();\n    }\n\n    #[test]\n    fn cross_workspace_no_known_workspaces_returns_zero() {\n        let dir = tempfile::tempdir().unwrap();\n        let global_path = #[test]\n    fn cross_workspace_empty_path_returns_zero() {\n        let dir = tempfile::tempdir().unwrap();\n        let other = tempfile::tempdir().unwrap();\n        write_learnings(\n DEFAULT_EXTRACTION_PROMPT: &str = r#\"You are analyzing a completed software task.","+Based on the title and close body below, write a concise retrospective section.","+","+Title: {title}","+Close type recurs, the key pattern to apply>","+\"#;","+","+// ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────","+// CliReflectAgent","+// ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────","+","+/// Production `ReflectAgent` that shells out to a CLI agent (e.g., `claude`).","+///","+/// The agent is invoked with the prompt fed via stdin redirection. The prompt","+/// is built by substituting `{title}` and `{close_body}` in the template.","+pub struct CliReflectAgent {","+    /// Agent binary name or path (e.g., `\"claude\"`).","+    agent_cmd: String,","+    /// Optional custom prompt template. Uses `DEFAULT_EXTRACTION_PROMPT` if None.","+    prompt_template: Option<String>,","+}","+","+impl CliReflectAgent {","+    /// Create a new `CliReflectAgent`.","+    ///","+    /// `agent_cmd` is the }","+}","+","+#[async_trait::async_trait]","+impl ReflectAgent for CliReflectAgent {","+    async fn extract_retrospective(","+        &self,","+        bead_title: &str,","+        close_body: &str,","+        workspace: &Path,","+    ) -> Result<Option<Retrospective>> {","+        // Build the prompt by substituting template variables.","+        let template = self","+            .prompt_template","+            .as_deref()","+            .unwrap_or(DEFAULT_EXTRACTION_PROMPT);","+        let prompt = template","+            .replace(\"{title}\", bead_title)","+            .replace(\"{close_body}\", close_body);","+","+        // Write the prompt to a temp file.","+        let tmp_path = std::path::PathBuf::from(format!(","+            \"/tmp/needle-reflect-{}.md\",","+            std::process::id()","+        ));","+        std::fs::write(&tmp_path, prompt)","+            .with_context(|| format!(\"failed to write reflect prompt to {}\", tmp_path.display()))?;","+","+        // Run the agent: cd into workspace, pipe prompt to agent.","+        let cmd = format!(","+            \"cd {} && {} < {}\",","+            workspace.display(),","+            self.agent_cmd,","+            tmp_path.display()","+        );","+","+        let output = tokio::process::Command::new(\"bash\")","+            .arg(\"-c\")","+            .arg(&cmd)","+            .output()","+            .await","+            .with_context(|| format!(\"failed to spawn reflect agent: {}\", self.agent_cmd))?;","+","+        // Always clean up the temp file.","+        let _ = std::fs::remove_file(&tmp_path);","+","+        if !output.status.success() {","+            anyhow::bail!(","+                \"reflect agent exited with code {}\",","+                output.status.code().unwrap_or(-1)","+            );","+        }","+","+        let stdout = String::from_utf8_lossy(&output.stdout);","+ Reflect strand: meta-analysis and learning consolidation.\n//!\n//! Strand 7 in the waterfall. Runs after all other strands return NoWork.\n//! This is the last productive strategy before giving up — meta-analysis\n//! only runs when there is genuinely nothing else to do.\n//!\n//! KAIROS-inspired four-phase cycle:\n//! 1. **Orient** — read current learnings.md and existing skills, check sizes.\n//! 2. **Gather** — read bead close bodies from issues.jsonl since last\n//!    consolidation; read traces for failed beads.\n//! 3. **Consolidate** — extract retrospective blocks, identify cross-bead\n//!    patterns, merge into learnings.md, deduplicate, resolve contradictions.\n//!    Promote learnings with reinforcement_count ≥ 3 to skill files.\n//! 4. **Prune** — remove entries older than `learning_retention_days` days\n//!    without reinforcement, compress similar entries, enforce `max_learnings`.\n//!\n//! Entry conditions (checked before running):\n//! - `strands.reflect.enabled` is true\n//! - 10+ beads closed since last consolidation (configurable)\n//! - 24+ hours since last consolidation (configurable cooldown)\n//!\n//! Guardrails:\n//! - Max `max_learnings_per_run` new learnings added per run\n//! - Max `max_skills_per_run` skill files created/updated per run\n//! - CLAUDE.md is read-only — never written\n//!\n//! Depends on: `config`, `learning`, `telemetry`, `types`.\n\nuse std::path::{Path, PathBuf};\n\nuse anyhow::{Context, Result};\nuse chrono::{DateTime, Utc};\nuse serde::{Deserialize, Serialize};\n\nuse
